<!-- id: p000024 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 公开招标公告
EN: Public Tender Announcement

<!-- id: p000025 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 项目概况
EN: Project Overview

<!-- id: p000026 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 新疆警察学院网络空间安全综合实验室建设项目（三次）的潜在投标人应在政采云平台https://www.zcygov.cn/在线申请获取招标文件，并于2025年7月31日 11:00（北京时间）前递交投标文件。
EN: Prospective bidders for the Xinjiang Police College Cyberspace Security Comprehensive Laboratory Construction Project (Third Tender) shall obtain the tender documents by applying online via the Government Procurement Cloud platform at https://www.zcygov.cn/ and shall submit bidding documents by 11:00 (Beijing Time) on July 31, 2025.

<!-- id: p000027 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 一、项目基本情况
EN: I. Basic Project Information

<!-- id: p000028 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 项目编号：XJNS-2025-HW-006-2
EN: Project No.: XJNS-2025-HW-006-2

<!-- id: p000029 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 项目名称：新疆警察学院网络空间安全综合实验室建设项目（三次）
EN: Project Name: Xinjiang Police College Cyberspace Security Comprehensive Laboratory Construction Project (Third Tender)

<!-- id: p000030 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 采购方式：公开招标
EN: Procurement Method: Open Tender

<!-- id: p000031 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 预算金额（元）：3700000.00
EN: Budget (CNY): 3700000.00

<!-- id: p000032 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 最高限价（元）：3700000.00
EN: Maximum Price Limit (CNY): 3700000.00

<!-- id: p000033 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 采购需求：网络空间安全综合实验室建设（详见招标文件）。
EN: Procurement Requirement: Construction of a cyberspace security comprehensive laboratory (see tender documents for details).

<!-- id: p000034 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 本项目（否）接受联合体投标。
EN: This project does (No) accept joint venture bids.

<!-- id: p000035 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 二、申请人的资格要求：
EN: II. Qualification Requirements for Applicants:

<!-- id: p000036 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 1.满足《中华人民共和国政府采购法》第二十二条规定；
EN: 1. Meet the requirements of Article 22 of the Government Procurement Law of the People’s Republic of China;

<!-- id: p000037 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （1）具有独立承担民事责任的能力；
EN: (1) Have the capacity to independently bear civil liability;

<!-- id: p000038 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （2）具有良好的商业信誉和健全的财务会计制度；
EN: (2) Have good business reputation and a sound financial and accounting system;

<!-- id: p000039 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （3）具有履行合同所必需的设备和专业技术能力；
EN: (3) Have the equipment and professional/technical capability necessary to perform the contract;

<!-- id: p000040 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （4）有依法缴纳税收和社会保障资金的良好记录；
EN: (4) Have a good record of paying taxes and social security contributions in accordance with law;

<!-- id: p000041 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （5）参加政府采购活动前三年内，在经营活动中没有重大违法记录；
EN: (5) Have no major illegal record in business activities within the three years prior to participation in government procurement activities;

<!-- id: p000042 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （6）法律、行政法规规定的其他条件。
EN: (6) Other conditions stipulated by laws and administrative regulations.

<!-- id: p000043 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2.落实政府采购政策需满足的资格要求：本项目不专门面向中小企业。
EN: 2. Qualification requirements for implementing government procurement policies: This project is not specifically oriented toward small and medium-sized enterprises.

<!-- id: p000044 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 3.本项目的特定资格要求：
EN: 3. Specific qualification requirements for this project:

<!-- id: p000045 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （1）、单位负责人为同一人或者存在直接控股、管理关系的不同供应商，不得参加同一标项下的政府采购活动。
EN: (1) Different suppliers whose person in charge is the same individual, or that have direct controlling or management relationships, may not participate in government procurement activities under the same bid item.

<!-- id: p000046 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 三、获取招标文件
EN: III. Obtaining Tender Documents

<!-- id: p000047 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 时间：2025年7月10日至2025年7月17日，每天上午00:00至12:00，下午12:00至23:59（北京时间，法定节假日除外）
EN: Time: July 10, 2025 to July 17, 2025; daily 00:00–12:00 and 12:00–23:59 (Beijing Time), excluding statutory holidays

<!-- id: p000048 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 地点：政采云平台https://www.zcygov.cn/在线申请
EN: Location: Government Procurement Cloud platform https://www.zcygov.cn/ (online application)

<!-- id: p000049 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 方式：投标人登录政采云平台https://www.zcygov.cn/在线申请获取采购文件（进入“项目采购”应用，在获取采购文件菜单中选择项目，申请获取采购文件）
EN: Method: Bidders log in to the Government Procurement Cloud platform https://www.zcygov.cn/ to apply online for procurement documents (enter the “Project Procurement” application, select the project under the “Obtain Procurement Documents” menu, and apply to obtain the procurement documents).

<!-- id: p000050 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 四、提交投标文件截止时间、开标时间和地点
EN: IV. Bid Submission Deadline; Bid Opening Time and Venue

<!-- id: p000051 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 提交投标文件截止时间：2025年7月31日 11:00（北京时间）
EN: Bid Submission Deadline: 11:00 on July 31, 2025 (Beijing Time)

<!-- id: p000052 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 投标地点：新疆政府采购网（http://www.ccgp-xinjiang.gov.cn）政采云线上平台
EN: Bid Submission Site: Xinjiang Government Procurement Network (http://www.ccgp-xinjiang.gov.cn) Government Procurement Cloud online platform

<!-- id: p000053 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 开标时间：2025年7月31日 11:00（北京时间）
EN: Bid Opening Time: 11:00 on July 31, 2025 (Beijing Time)

<!-- id: p000054 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 开标地点：新疆政府采购网（http://www.ccgp-xinjiang.gov.cn）政采云线上平台
EN: Bid Opening Venue: Xinjiang Government Procurement Network (http://www.ccgp-xinjiang.gov.cn) Government Procurement Cloud online platform

<!-- id: p000055 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 五、公告期限
EN: V. Announcement Period

<!-- id: p000056 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 自本公告发布之日起5个工作日。
EN: 5 working days from the date this announcement is published.

<!-- id: p000057 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 六、其他补充事宜
EN: VI. Other Supplementary Matters

<!-- id: p000058 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （1）、本项目实行电子招投标，供应商须登录政采云平台申请获取采购文件，并通过政采云电子投标客户端制作响应文件，同时自行承担与投标有关的一切费用。
EN: (1) This project implements electronic bidding. Suppliers must log in to the Government Procurement Cloud platform to apply for procurement documents and prepare response documents using the Government Procurement Cloud electronic bidding client, and shall bear all costs related to bidding.

<!-- id: p000059 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （2）、各供应商应在开标前确保成为新疆维吾尔自治区政府采购网正式注册入库供应商，并完成CA数字证书申领。因未注册入库、未办理CA数字证书等原因造成无法投标或投标失败等后果由供应商自行承担。
EN: (2) Before bid opening, each supplier shall ensure it is formally registered and on file as a supplier on the Xinjiang Uyghur Autonomous Region Government Procurement Network, and complete application for a CA digital certificate. Any consequences such as inability to bid or bid failure due to not being registered/on file or not obtaining a CA digital certificate shall be borne by the supplier.

<!-- id: p000060 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （3）、有意向参与新疆区域电子开评标的供应商，可访问新疆数字证书认证中心官方网站（https://www.xjca.com.cn/）或下载“新疆政务通”APP自行进行申领。如需咨询，请联系新疆CA服务热线0991-2819290。
EN: (3) Suppliers intending to participate in Xinjiang-region electronic bid opening and evaluation may visit the official website of the Xinjiang Digital Certificate Authentication Center (https://www.xjca.com.cn/) or download the “Xinjiang Government Services” app to apply. For consultation, please contact the Xinjiang CA service hotline 0991-2819290.

<!-- id: p000061 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （4）、供应商可前往新疆政府采购网（http://www.ccgp-xinjiang.gov.cn/）下载专区，下载政采云电子投标客户端，安装完成后，可通过账号密码或CA登录客户端进行响应文件制作。在使用政采云电子投标客户端时，建议使用WIN7及以上操作系统。如有问题可拨打政采云客户服务热线95763进行咨询。
EN: (4) Suppliers may go to the download section of the Xinjiang Government Procurement Network (http://www.ccgp-xinjiang.gov.cn/) to download the Government Procurement Cloud electronic bidding client. After installation, suppliers may log in via account/password or CA to prepare response documents. When using the Government Procurement Cloud electronic bidding client, it is recommended to use WIN7 or above. For issues, call the Government Procurement Cloud customer service hotline 95763.

<!-- id: p000062 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （5）、本项目采用不见面开标，供应商须在投标截止时间前通过CA在政采云平台上传加密的电子响应文件。备注：供应商对不见面开评标系统的技术操作咨询，可通过https://edu.zcygov.cn/luban/xinjiang-e-biding自助查询，也可在政采云帮助中心常见问题解答和操作流程讲解视频中自助查询，网址为：https://service.zcygov.cn/#/help，“项目采购”—“操作流程-电子招投标”—“政府采购项目电子交易管理操作指南-供应商”版面获取操作指南，同时对自助查询无法解决的问题可通过钉钉群及政采云在线客服获取服务支持。
EN: (5) This project adopts non-face-to-face bid opening. Suppliers must upload the encrypted electronic response documents on the Government Procurement Cloud platform via CA before the bid deadline. Note: For technical operation consultation regarding the non-face-to-face bid opening and evaluation system, suppliers may self-check via https://edu.zcygov.cn/luban/xinjiang-e-biding, or self-check via the Government Procurement Cloud Help Center FAQs and operation walkthrough videos at https://service.zcygov.cn/#/help under “Project Procurement” → “Operation Process – Electronic Bidding” → “Government Procurement Project Electronic Transaction Management Operation Guide – Supplier,” and for issues not resolved through self-check, obtain support via the DingTalk group and Government Procurement Cloud online customer service.

<!-- id: p000063 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （6）、供应商在开标前须提前配置好电脑浏览器（建议使用360浏览器或谷歌浏览器），开标时请使用制作加密电子响应文件的CA锁进行解密及报价确认。本项目响应文件解密时间定为30分钟，如因自身原因导致无法正常解密，后果由供应商自行承担。
EN: (6) Before bid opening, suppliers must configure their computer browser in advance (360 Browser or Google Chrome is recommended). At bid opening, please use the CA token used to produce the encrypted electronic response document to decrypt and confirm the quotation. The decryption time for response documents in this project is set to 30 minutes; if decryption cannot be completed normally due to the supplier’s own reasons, the consequences shall be borne by the supplier.

<!-- id: p000064 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （7）、响应文件开启当日，供应商无需到达开标现场，仅需通过政采云平台“不见面”开标大厅完成远程解密、开标唱标、询标澄清、在线多轮报价、结果公布等交互环节。供应商必须使用能正确解密响应文件的“CA锁”在规定的时间内完成远程解密，因供应商因未能解密、解密失败或解密超时，视为供应商撤销其响应文件。
EN: (7) On the day response documents are opened, suppliers do not need to arrive at the bid opening site; they only need to complete interactive steps such as remote decryption, bid opening announcement, inquiry and clarification, online multi-round quotation, and result publication through the “non-face-to-face” bid opening hall on the Government Procurement Cloud platform. Suppliers must use a “CA token” that can correctly decrypt the response documents to complete remote decryption within the prescribed time; if the supplier fails to decrypt, decryption fails, or decryption times out, it shall be deemed that the supplier has withdrawn its response document.

<!-- id: p000065 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （8）、逾期上传或者未上传指定地点的响应文件，采购人不予受理。
EN: (8) Response documents uploaded late or not uploaded to the designated location will not be accepted by the purchaser.

<!-- id: p000066 type: paragraph -->

EN: VII. For inquiries about this procurement, please contact as follows

Qualification requirements for implementing government procurement policies: this project is not specifically oriented toward small and medium-sized enterprises.<br/>3. ZH_ROW: | 12 | 报价方式 | 一次报价。为交钥匙项目。<br/>报价应包含招标文件中所有费用：包括所需设备报价（含税金）、运输费、装卸费、保管、搬运、安装、调试、验收、拆装、培训、备品备件、保险、售后服务、税款、测试、质检、检验、行政许可及相关证书等直至交付采购人正常使用前的一切费用。（以上内容包含但不限于）<br/>采购人质保期内不再支付任何与项目有关的费用（包含维护维修、设备非人为原因更换等。） |
EN_ROW: | 12 | Quotation method | One-time quotation. This is a turnkey project.<br/>The quotation shall include all costs in the tender documents, including (but not limited to) required equipment prices (including taxes), transportation, loading/unloading, storage, handling, installation, commissioning, acceptance, disassembly/reassembly, training, spare parts, insurance, after-sales service, taxes, testing, quality inspection, examination, administrative permits and related certificates, etc., up to all costs before delivery to the purchaser for normal use.<br/>During the warranty period, the purchaser will not pay any additional expenses related to the project (including maintenance/repairs, replacement of equipment due to non-human causes, etc.). |

<!-- id: t000014 type: table_row -->

EN_ROW: | 13 | Payment method | Within 7 days after the contract is signed, Party A shall pay Party B an advance payment of 40% of the total contract price. Within 7 days after all items procured by Party A arrive and pass inspection/acceptance, Party A shall pay Party B 30% of the total contract price. Within 7 days after all goods are installed and commissioned and pass Party A’s acceptance, Party A shall pay Party B 30% of the total contract price. (The specific payment method shall be agreed with Party A when signing the contract.) |

<!-- id: p000079 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 第二部分  投标人须知
EN: Part II  Instructions to Bidders

<!-- id: p000080 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 1、适用范围
EN: 1. Scope of Application

<!-- id: p000081 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 招标文件是采购人在本项目投标过程中的规范性文件，仅适用于本次招标中所叙述项目的货物及安装服务采购等内容。和采购人组织的答疑纪要一起是各投标人（以下简称投标人）编制投标文件的依据，也是采购人与中标人签订合同的依据，并作为供货合同的附件之一，与供货合同具有同等的法律效力（除非合同另有约定的部分，以正式合同内容为准）。
EN: The tender documents are normative documents of the purchaser in the bidding process for this project and apply only to the procurement of goods and installation services for the project described in this tender. Together with any Q&A minutes organized by the purchaser, they serve as the basis for each bidder (hereinafter “bidder”) to prepare bidding documents, and as the basis for the purchaser to sign a contract with the winning bidder. They also constitute an attachment to the supply contract and have the same legal effect as the supply contract (except where the contract separately provides otherwise; the formal contract terms prevail).

<!-- id: p000082 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2、定义
EN: 2. Definitions

<!-- id: p000083 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 下列术语和缩写的定义为：
EN: The definitions of the following terms and abbreviations are:

<!-- id: p000084 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2.1  “采购人”系指对本招标文件中所列货物有需求的新疆警察学院（新疆公安警察培训基地）；“投标人”系指符合招标文件要求并且通过资格审查进入招标程序的投标人；采购代理机构”系指新疆能实建设工程项目管理咨询有限责任公司；“投标文件”系指投标人为响应招标文件而编制、递交的投标文件。
EN: 2.1 “Purchaser” refers to Xinjiang Police College (Xinjiang Public Security Police Training Base), which has demand for the goods listed in these tender documents; “Bidder” refers to a bidder that meets the requirements of the tender documents and has passed qualification review and entered the tendering procedure; “Procurement agent” refers to Xinjiang Nengshi Construction Project Management Consulting Co., Ltd.; and “Bidding documents” refer to the bidding documents prepared and submitted by the bidder in response to the tender documents.

<!-- id: p000085 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2.2  “买方”系新疆警察学院（新疆公安警察培训基地），“卖方”系指中标投标人。
EN: 2.2 “Buyer” refers to Xinjiang Police College (Xinjiang Public Security Police Training Base), and “Seller” refers to the winning bidder.

<!-- id: p000086 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2.3 “合同”系指买卖双方签署规定的，买卖双方权利与义务的协议，以及所有的附件、附录和投标文件所提到的构成合同的所有文件。
EN: 2.3 “Contract” refers to the agreement signed by the buyer and seller specifying the rights and obligations of both parties, as well as all annexes, appendices, and all documents that constitute the contract as referenced in the bidding documents.

<!-- id: p000087 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2.4  “货物”系指卖方按招标文件规定须向买方提供的货物所需一切设备、 软件系统、手册及其它有关说明资料和材料。
EN: 2.4 “Goods” refers to all equipment, software systems, manuals, and other relevant explanatory materials and documents required for the goods that the seller must provide to the buyer in accordance with the tender documents.

<!-- id: p000088 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2.5  “服务”系指根据本合同规定卖方必须承担的安装、调试、技术协助、 技术培训以及其他类似的附随义务。
EN: 2.5 “Services” refers to installation, commissioning, technical assistance, technical training, and other similar incidental obligations that the seller must undertake pursuant to this contract.

<!-- id: p000089 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2.6  “附随服务”系指根据本合同规定卖方必须承担与货物有关的辅助服务， 如送货上门、免费维护以及合同中规定卖方应承担的义务，以及合同中未规定， 但依有利于合同履行原则，应当由卖方承担的其它义务。
EN: 2.6 “Incidental services” refers to auxiliary services related to the goods that the seller must undertake under this contract, such as delivery to the site, free maintenance, and obligations the seller must undertake as stipulated in the contract, as well as other obligations not specified in the contract but that, under the principle of facilitating contract performance, should be borne by the seller.

<!-- id: p000090 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 3、投标费用
EN: 3. Bidding Costs

<!-- id: p000091 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 3.1  无论投标结果如何，与参与招标、投标活动有关的所有费用将由投标人自行承担。
EN: 3.1 Regardless of the bid outcome, all costs related to participating in the tendering and bidding activities shall be borne by the bidder.

<!-- id: p000092 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 3.2  投标人被视为熟悉本采购项目的各种情况以及履行合同有关的一切情况。
EN: 3.2 The bidder shall be deemed to be familiar with all circumstances of this procurement project and all circumstances related to performance of the contract.

<!-- id: p000093 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 3.3  投标人应承担其编制投标文件与递交投标文件所涉及的一切费用，不论投标结果如何，采购人对上述费用不做任何补偿。
EN: 3.3 The bidder shall bear all costs involved in preparing and submitting the bidding documents. Regardless of the bid outcome, the purchaser will not provide any compensation for the above costs.

<!-- id: p000094 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 3.4  与相关联工作间的联系协调工作，如有费用发生已包含在投标价格内。
EN: 3.4 Any liaison and coordination work with related work, if any costs arise, has already been included in the bid price.

<!-- id: p000095 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4、招标文件的构成
EN: 4. Composition of the Tender Documents

<!-- id: p000096 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.1  招标文件由下述部分组成
EN: 4.1 The tender documents consist of the following parts:

<!-- id: p000097 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 第一部分  投标人须知前附表
EN: Part I  Instructions to Bidders – Front Appendix

<!-- id: p000098 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 第二部分  投标人须知
EN: Part II  Instructions to Bidders

<!-- id: p000099 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 第三部分  投标说明
EN: Part III  Bidding Instructions

<!-- id: p000100 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 第四部分  采购货物清单及技术规格要求
EN: Part IV  List of Procured Goods and Technical Specification Requirements

<!-- id: p000101 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 第五部分  合同条款
EN: Part V  Contract Terms

<!-- id: p000102 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 第六部分  附 表
EN: Part VI  Appendices

<!-- id: p000103 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 第七部分  评定办法和细则
EN: Part VII  Evaluation Methods and Detailed Rules

<!-- id: p000104 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.2  一切有效的招标文件的澄清和修改的书面文件均是招标文件不可分割的部分。
EN: 4.2 All valid written documents of clarification and amendment to the tender documents are an inseparable part of the tender documents.

<!-- id: p000105 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5. 招标文件的澄清
EN: 5. Clarification of the Tender Documents

<!-- id: p000106 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.1  招标文件中的标题或题名仅起引导作用，而不应视为对招标文件内容的理解和解释。
EN: 5.1 The titles or headings in the tender documents are for guidance only and shall not be regarded as understanding or interpretation of the contents of the tender documents.

<!-- id: p000107 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.2  除非有特殊要求，招标文件不单独提供招标货物使用地的自然环境、气候条件、公用设施等情况，投标人被视为熟悉上述与履行合同有关的一切情况。
EN: 5.2 Unless otherwise specially required, the tender documents do not separately provide information on the natural environment, climate conditions, public utilities, etc. of the place where the tendered goods will be used. The bidder shall be deemed to be familiar with all of the above circumstances related to performance of the contract.

<!-- id: p000108 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.3  招标文件的解释权归招标人和招标代理机构。
EN: 5.3 The right to interpret the tender documents belongs to the tenderer and the procurement agent.

<!-- id: p000109 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.4  任何要求对招标文件进行澄清的投标人，均应将需澄清的内容以书面形式或扫描件送达采购代理机构，采购代理机构将予以答复（答复中不包括问题的来源），答复内容将发送投标人联系邮箱，不再另行通知，请各投标人务必关注联系邮箱，否则，所造成的一切风险由投标人自行承担。
EN: 5.4 Any bidder requesting clarification of the tender documents shall deliver the matters requiring clarification to the procurement agent in written form or as scanned copies. The procurement agent will reply (without indicating the source of the question). The reply will be sent to the bidder’s contact email, and no separate notice will be issued. All bidders must pay attention to their contact email; otherwise, all risks arising therefrom shall be borne by the bidder.

<!-- id: p000110 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.5  为了使投标人有足够的时间准备投标文件,各投标人须在投标人须知前附表中规定的时间前(超过该时间收到的需澄清的内容,采购代理机构有权不予答复），准备需澄清的内容，以书面形式送达采购代理机构。
EN: 5.5 In order to allow bidders sufficient time to prepare the bidding documents, each bidder must prepare the matters requiring clarification and deliver them to the procurement agent in written form before the time specified in the front appendix to the Instructions to Bidders (for clarification requests received after that time, the procurement agent has the right not to respond).

<!-- id: p000111 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 6、招标文件的修改或补充
EN: 6. Amendment or Supplement to the Tender Documents

<!-- id: p000112 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 6.1  特殊情形的，在递交投标文件截止期15日前，采购代理机构可主动地或在解答投标人提出的澄清问题时对招标文件进行澄清和修改。
EN: 6.1 In special circumstances, no later than 15 days before the deadline for submission of bidding documents, the procurement agent may, on its own initiative, or when replying to bidders’ clarification questions, issue clarifications and amendments to the tender documents.

<!-- id: p000113 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 6.2  招标文件的澄清和修改将以书面公布的形式通知所有购买招标文件的投标人，并对其具有约束力。
EN: 6.2 Clarifications and amendments to the tender documents will be notified to all bidders who have obtained the tender documents in written published form, and shall be binding upon them.

<!-- id: p000114 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 6.3  为使投标人在准备投标文件时有充分的时间对招标文件的澄清和修改部分进行研究，采购代理机构可在递交投标文件截止期15日前通知投标人，适当延长递交投标文件截止期。
EN: 6.3 In order to give bidders sufficient time to study the clarification and amendment parts when preparing bidding documents, the procurement agent may, no later than 15 days before the deadline for submission of bidding documents, notify bidders and appropriately extend the submission deadline.

<!-- id: p000115 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 6.4  招标文件的澄清和修改文件是招标文件的组成部分，投标人需按照招标文件的澄清和修改文件的要求参与招标，投标人没有作出实质性响应是投标人的风险，并可能导致其投标文件被拒绝。
EN: 6.4 The clarification and amendment documents are part of the tender documents. Bidders shall participate in the tender in accordance with the requirements of such clarification and amendment documents. Failure to make a substantive response is the bidder’s risk and may cause its bidding documents to be rejected.

<!-- id: p000116 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 7、索赔
EN: 7. Claims

<!-- id: p000117 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 投标人提供的设备未能达到标书规定的性能要求，或者有明显缺陷及损坏的设备，采购人将保留退货索赔或提出更换新设备的权利。
EN: If the equipment provided by the bidder fails to meet the performance requirements specified in the tender documents, or if the equipment has obvious defects or damage, the purchaser reserves the right to return the goods for a claim, or to request replacement with new equipment.

<!-- id: p000118 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 8、验收
EN: 8. Acceptance

<!-- id: p000119 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 8.1  投标人所售出的设备运抵买方指定的交货地点，由买卖双方共同对设备型号、规格、数量、外观、包装及资料。文件（如装箱单、质保单、随箱介质等）验收，并清点登记。
EN: 8.1 After the equipment sold by the bidder is delivered to the delivery location designated by the buyer, the buyer and seller shall jointly inspect and accept the equipment model, specifications, quantity, appearance, packaging, and accompanying materials/documents (such as packing list, warranty certificate, accompanying media, etc.), and conduct counting and registration.

<!-- id: p000120 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 8.2  验收标准：按国家，行业技术标准和规范，招标文件的质量要求和技术指标、中标人的投标文件及承诺进行验收，最终须达到采购人使用要求。
EN: 8.2 Acceptance standards: Acceptance shall be conducted in accordance with national and industry technical standards and specifications, the quality requirements and technical indicators in the tender documents, and the winning bidder’s bidding documents and commitments, and the final result must meet the purchaser’s usage requirements.

<!-- id: p000121 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 9、产品售后服务要求
EN: 9. Product After-Sales Service Requirements

<!-- id: p000122 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 9.1  质量与售后服务、技术指标要求：投标人应保证其提供的货物是全新的、未使用过的，并在各个方面符合合同规定的质量、规格和性能要求。在规定的质量保证期内，卖方应对由于设计、工艺或材料的缺陷而造成的故障负责。投标人应免费负责修理或更换有缺陷的零部件或整机，承担质保的责任。
EN: 9.1 Requirements for quality, after-sales service, and technical indicators: The bidder shall ensure that the goods it provides are brand new and unused, and conform in all respects to the quality, specifications, and performance requirements stipulated in the contract. During the specified quality warranty period, the seller shall be responsible for failures caused by defects in design, workmanship, or materials. The bidder shall repair or replace defective parts or the whole unit free of charge and bear the warranty responsibilities.

<!-- id: p000123 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 9.2  投标人应保证招标文件中涉及到的所有内容，不会出现因第三方提出侵犯其专利权、商标权或其它知识产权而引发法律或经济纠纷，否则由投标人承担全部责任，投标人须拥有所招标的物的所有权或合法处分权，一切因标的物的所有权或合法处分权而引起的法律和经济纠纷由投标人自行负责，与本项目采购代理机构、采购人无关。
EN: 9.2 The bidder shall ensure that all contents involved in the tender documents will not give rise to legal or economic disputes due to any third party alleging infringement of its patent rights, trademark rights, or other intellectual property rights; otherwise, the bidder shall bear full responsibility. The bidder must have ownership of, or lawful right of disposition over, the tendered items. All legal and economic disputes arising from ownership of, or lawful right of disposition over, the subject matter shall be borne by the bidder, and are unrelated to the procurement agent and the purchaser of this project.

<!-- id: p000124 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 9.3  投标人提供的设备应运行安全可靠，使用寿命长，维护费用低。
EN: 9.3 The equipment provided by the bidder shall operate safely and reliably, have a long service life, and have low maintenance costs.

<!-- id: p000125 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 9.4  投标人应负责将货物运至合同中规定的现场，并派工程技术人员进行设备安装、调试，保证正常使用。安装完毕后投标人应派专业技术人员应对采购人的技术人员进行使用操作、维修、保养等技术的现场培训，直至采购人的技术人员能熟练独立工作。投标人委派的专业技术人员所需费均由投标人自行承担。
EN: 9.4 The bidder shall be responsible for transporting the goods to the site specified in the contract and dispatch engineering and technical personnel to install and commission the equipment to ensure normal use. After installation is completed, the bidder shall dispatch professional technical personnel to provide on-site training to the purchaser’s technical personnel on operation, repair, maintenance, etc., until the purchaser’s technical personnel can work proficiently and independently. All expenses required for the professional technical personnel dispatched by the bidder shall be borne by the bidder.

<!-- id: p000126 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 9.5  服务期间如出现无法确定的故障，投标人要协同解决故障，不得以任何理由相互推诿。质保期后，要求能提供广泛、及时、优惠的技术服务及时提供质量可靠的各种配件。
EN: 9.5 If an indeterminate fault occurs during the service period, the bidder shall cooperate in resolving the fault and shall not shirk responsibility for any reason. After the warranty period, the bidder is required to provide broad, timely, and favorable technical services, and to timely provide various quality-reliable spare parts.

<!-- id: p000127 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 9.6  产品售后服务要求：1）中标方在质保期内应对所供货物提供现场免费保修（技术参数中有要求的以技术参数要求为准）。保修期内，非因操作不当造成要更换的零配件及货物由中标方负责包修、包换。在质保期结束前1个月，中标方须免费对货物进行一次全面的维护与保养。
EN: 9.6 Product after-sales service requirements: 1) During the warranty period, the winning bidder shall provide on-site free warranty for the supplied goods (where the technical parameters specify requirements, those requirements shall prevail). During the warranty period, spare parts and goods that need replacement not caused by improper operation shall be repaired/replaced by the winning bidder. One month before the end of the warranty period, the winning bidder shall perform one comprehensive maintenance and servicing of the goods free of charge.

<!-- id: p000128 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2）中标方应在产品全生命周期内提供技术咨询服务工作，并随时提供技术支持和有关技术资料。
EN: 2) The winning bidder shall provide technical consulting services throughout the entire product lifecycle, and provide technical support and relevant technical documentation at any time.

<!-- id: p000129 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 3）维修服务响应
EN: 3) Repair service response

<!-- id: p000130 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 质量保修期内要求中标方到达现场进行免费维修服务，一般故障4小时内解决，重大故障24小时内解决。故障原因24小时内无法排除的，则应提供相应备用设备以保证用户方正常使用。
EN: During the quality warranty period, the winning bidder is required to arrive on site to provide free repair services. General faults shall be resolved within 4 hours, and major faults shall be resolved within 24 hours. If the cause of the fault cannot be eliminated within 24 hours, corresponding backup equipment shall be provided to ensure normal use by the user.

<!-- id: p000131 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4）投标方可视自身能力在投标文件中提供更优、更合理的维修服务承诺。
EN: 4) The bidder may, depending on its capabilities, provide better and more reasonable repair service commitments in the bidding documents.

<!-- id: p000132 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5）质保期结束以后，投标人仍需提供优质服务，进行定期维护与修理，并仅收取成本费（包括零配件）。投标人在投标文件中必须明确承诺。
EN: 5) After the warranty period ends, the bidder shall still provide high-quality services, perform regular maintenance and repairs, and charge only the cost (including spare parts). The bidder must make a clear commitment in the bidding documents.

<!-- id: p000133 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 9.7  投标人应充分考虑现场环境条件，并提供配套的设备，所投设备必须达到国家强制性安全要求、及相关标准。
EN: 9.7 The bidder shall fully consider the on-site environmental conditions and provide supporting equipment. The offered equipment must meet national mandatory safety requirements and relevant standards.

<!-- id: p000134 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 9.8  随机资料及随机配件齐全。
EN: 9.8 The accompanying documentation and accessories shall be complete.

<!-- id: p000135 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 10、保密
EN: 10. Confidentiality

<!-- id: p000136 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 招投标双方应为对方在投标文件和招标文件中涉及的商业和技术等秘密保密，违者应对由此造成的后果承担一切责任。
EN: Both parties to the tender and bid shall keep confidential the other party’s business, technical, and other secrets involved in the bidding documents and tender documents. Violators shall bear all responsibility for the consequences caused thereby.

<!-- id: p000137 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 11、代理服务费
EN: 11. Agency Service Fee

<!-- id: p000138 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 服务费收费标准参考国家发展计划委员会文件（计价格[2002]1980号文）执行，由中标人支付。（附：招标代理收费标准）
EN: The service fee charging standard shall be implemented by reference to the document of the State Development Planning Commission (Ji Jia Ge [2002] No. 1980), and shall be paid by the winning bidder. (Appendix: Tender agency fee charging standards)

<!-- id: t000035 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: | 招标类别<br/>中标价（万） | 货物招标取费标准 | 服务招标取费标准 | 工程招标取费标准 |
EN_ROW: | Tender category<br/>Winning price (10,000 CNY) | Fee rate for goods tenders | Fee rate for service tenders | Fee rate for construction tenders |

<!-- id: t000036 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: | 100以下 | 1.5% | 1.5% | 1.0% |
EN_ROW: | Below 100 | 1.5% | 1.5% | 1.0% |

EN_ROW: | 100–500 | 1.1% | 0.8% | 0.7% |

<!-- id: t000038 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: | 500-1000 | 0.8% | 0.45% | 0.55% |
EN_ROW: | 500–1000 | 0.8% | 0.45% | 0.55% |

<!-- id: t000039 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: | 1000-5000 | 0.5% | 0.25% | 0.35% |
EN_ROW: | 1000–5000 | 0.5% | 0.25% | 0.35% |

<!-- id: t000040 type: table_row -->

EN_ROW: | 5000–10000 | 0.25% | 0.1% | 0.2% |
