<!-- id: p000139 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 注：招标代理服务收费按差额定率累进法计算。
EN: Note: Tender agency service fees are calculated using the differential rate progressive method.

<!-- id: p000140 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 第三部分  投标说明
EN: Part III  Bidding Instructions

<!-- id: p000141 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 第一章  投标人资格要求
EN: Chapter 1  Bidder Qualification Requirements

<!-- id: p000142 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 1、投标资格
EN: 1. Bid Qualification

<!-- id: p000143 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 1.1  投标人必须提交能够证明其具有履行本项目合同能力的资质证明文件，作为投标文件的一部分。
EN: 1.1 The bidder must submit qualification supporting documents that can prove it has the ability to perform this project contract, as part of the bidding documents.

<!-- id: p000144 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 1.1.1  提供有效的营业执照等证明材料（加盖单位公章）；
EN: 1.1.1 Provide valid business license and other supporting materials (affixed with the company’s official seal);

<!-- id: p000145 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 1.1.2  提供 2023 年度或 2024 年度的会计报表或审计报告，包括资产负债表、利润表、现金流量表和财务情况说明书，复印件加盖公章。(成立不足 1 年的提供自成立以来的财务审计报告或财务报 表)；
EN: 1.1.2 Provide 2023 or 2024 financial statements or audit report, including the balance sheet, income statement, cash flow statement, and financial notes, with copies affixed with the official seal. (For entities established for less than 1 year, provide an audit report or financial statements since establishment);

<!-- id: p000146 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 1.1.3  根据项目需求提供履行合同所必需的设备和专业技术能力加盖公章的声明；
EN: 1.1.3 Provide a statement, affixed with the official seal, of the equipment and professional/technical capability necessary to perform the contract as required by the project;

<!-- id: p000147 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 1.1.4  提供近期 3 个月完税证明和近期 3 个月社会保险的凭据证明材料复印件加盖公章；如依法免税或不需要缴纳社会保障资金的，应提供相应文件证明；
EN: 1.1.4 Provide copies (with official seal) of proof of tax payment for the most recent 3 months and proof of social insurance for the most recent 3 months; if exempt from tax by law or not required to pay social security funds, provide corresponding documentary proof;

<!-- id: p000148 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 1.1.5  提供参加本次政府采购活动前3年内在经营活动中没有重大违法记录声明函（加盖公章）；
EN: 1.1.5 Provide a statement letter (affixed with official seal) that there has been no major illegal record in business operations within the 3 years prior to participation in this government procurement activity;

<!-- id: p000149 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 1.1.6 法人授权委托书或法人身份证明书，授权人或法人（法人参与投标时提供）有效身份证明；
EN: 1.1.6 Provide the legal representative’s authorization letter or legal representative identity certificate, and valid identification of the authorized person or the legal representative (provided when the legal representative participates in bidding);

<!-- id: p000150 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 1.1.7 提供承诺函：单位负责人为同一人或者存在直接控股、管理关系的不同投标人，未参加同一合同项下的政府采购活动。
EN: 1.1.7 Provide a commitment letter: different bidders whose person in charge is the same individual or that have direct controlling or management relationships have not participated in government procurement activities under the same contract item.

<!-- id: p000151 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 1.1.8 投标保证金交纳凭证；
EN: 1.1.8 Bid bond payment voucher;

<!-- id: p000152 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 注: 1、以上证明文件，都须在投标文件中放入加盖公章的复印件，所有内容的扫描件需上传至政采云系统，在开标资格审查时用于核对（有特别说明的除外），未上传的视为对招标文件资格审查内容的不响应，投标将被拒绝。
EN: Note: 1) The above supporting documents must be included in the bidding documents as copies affixed with the official seal. Scanned copies of all contents must be uploaded to the Government Procurement Cloud system for verification during bid-opening qualification review (unless otherwise specifically stated). Failure to upload will be deemed non-response to the qualification review contents of the tender documents, and the bid will be rejected.

<!-- id: p000153 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2、对有特别说明的不能上传以上营业执照及资质证书的，可上传法定有效的公证件。资格审查不合格或不能提供保证金证明时，将取消其投标资格。
EN: 2) Where specially stated that the above business license and qualification certificates cannot be uploaded, legally valid notarized documents may be uploaded. If qualification review is unqualified or bond proof cannot be provided, the bidding qualification will be cancelled.

<!-- id: p000154 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 第二章  投标文件的编写及编制顺序
EN: Chapter 2  Preparation of Bidding Documents and Order of Compilation

<!-- id: p000155 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2、要求
EN: 2. Requirements

<!-- id: p000156 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2.1  投标人应详细阅读招标文件中的条款、规范、表示、条件和格式等所有内容，按招标文件的要求份数提供投标文件，并保证所提供全部材料的真实性，以使其投标对招标文件做出实质性响应。否则，其投标会被拒绝。
EN: 2.1 The bidder shall read in detail all contents of the tender documents, including clauses, specifications, representations, conditions, formats, etc., provide bidding documents in the number of copies required by the tender documents, and ensure the authenticity of all materials provided, so that its bid makes a substantive response to the tender documents. Otherwise, its bid will be rejected.

<!-- id: p000157 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2.2  开标、评标、授标均以项目为单位，投标人根据公司的自身实力进行投标，并在所投项目密封袋上清楚标明所投项目的名称。
EN: 2.2 Bid opening, bid evaluation, and award are all conducted on a project basis. The bidder shall bid according to its own strength and clearly indicate the name of the bid project on the sealed package of the submitted project.

<!-- id: p000158 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 3、投标文件语言和度量单位
EN: 3. Language and Units of Measurement for Bidding Documents

<!-- id: p000159 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 3.1  招标文件及投标人和采购方就本次采购交换的文件和往来信件，须以中文书写。
EN: 3.1 The tender documents, and the documents and correspondence exchanged between the bidder and the purchaser regarding this procurement, shall be written in Chinese.

<!-- id: p000160 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 3.2  除在招标文件的技术规格中另有规定外，计量单位应使用中华人民共和国法定计量单位。
EN: 3.2 Unless otherwise specified in the technical specifications of the tender documents, the units of measurement shall be the legal units of measurement of the People’s Republic of China.

<!-- id: p000161 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4、投标文件的编制
EN: 4. Preparation of Bidding Documents

<!-- id: p000162 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.1  投标文件的构成
EN: 4.1 Composition of the Bidding Documents

<!-- id: p000163 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.1.1投标人应认真阅读招标文件的所有内容，按招标文件的要求提供投标文件，并保证提供的全部资料的真实性，以使其投标对招标文件作出实质性响应，否则，其投标将被拒绝。
EN: 4.1.1 The bidder shall carefully read all contents of the tender documents, provide bidding documents in accordance with the requirements of the tender documents, and ensure the authenticity of all information provided so that its bid makes a substantive response to the tender documents; otherwise, its bid will be rejected.

<!-- id: p000164 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.1.2 投标文件以不可拆解的方式装订文件，至少包含4.2-4.4三部分内容。
EN: 4.1.2 The bidding documents shall be bound in a non-detachable manner and shall include at least the three parts in Sections 4.2–4.4.

<!-- id: p000165 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.2  投标报价一览表
EN: 4.2 Summary Table of Bid Quotation

<!-- id: p000166 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.2.1 报价一览表（按附件的格式提供，正、副本中均应附入）。
EN: 4.2.1 Summary table of quotation (provided in the format of the attachment, and included in both the original and duplicate copies).

<!-- id: p000167 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.3  投标文件
EN: 4.3 Bidding Documents

<!-- id: p000168 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 投标人必须按要求如实、准确、完整的提供评估因素要求的各类文件资料。否则投标将不被接受。投标文件至少应包括以下部分（但不局限于以下内容及顺序）：
EN: The bidder must truthfully, accurately, and completely provide various documents and materials required by the evaluation factors as required. Otherwise, the bid will not be accepted. The bidding documents shall include at least the following parts (but are not limited to the following contents and order):

<!-- id: p000169 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.3.1承诺函；
EN: 4.3.1 Commitment letter;

<!-- id: p000170 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.3.2法定代表人身份证明及法定代表人授权委托书；
EN: 4.3.2 Legal representative identity certificate and legal representative authorization letter;

<!-- id: p000171 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.3.3投标报价一览表；
EN: 4.3.3 Summary table of bid quotation;

<!-- id: p000172 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.3.4明细报价表；
EN: 4.3.4 Detailed quotation table;

<!-- id: p000173 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.3.5投标人资格、资信证明文件；
EN: 4.3.5 Bidder qualification and credit supporting documents;

<!-- id: p000174 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.3.6 技术方案、实施方案、售后服务方案、应急服务方案；
EN: 4.3.6 Technical proposal, implementation plan, after-sales service plan, and emergency service plan;

<!-- id: p000175 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.3.7有关投标产品功能、技术性能详述；
EN: 4.3.7 Detailed description of the functions and technical performance of the bid products;

<!-- id: p000176 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.3.8 有关投标产品的质量证明材料等（根据实际情况提供）；
EN: 4.3.8 Quality certification materials for the bid products, etc. (provided as appropriate);

<!-- id: p000177 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.3.9 技术参数、功能偏离表；
EN: 4.3.9 Technical parameters and functional deviation table;

<!-- id: p000178 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.3.10商务条款偏离表；
EN: 4.3.10 Commercial terms deviation table;

<!-- id: p000179 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.3.11质量保证书；
EN: 4.3.11 Quality guarantee letter;

<!-- id: p000180 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.3.12其他有利于投标的资料；
EN: 4.3.12 Other materials favorable to the bid;

<!-- id: p000181 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.3.13投标单位反商业贿赂承诺书。
EN: 4.3.13 Bidder’s anti-commercial-bribery commitment letter.

<!-- id: p000182 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.4  投标文件格式
EN: 4.4 Format of the Bidding Documents

<!-- id: p000183 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.4.1 本项目要求按照上述内容编制标书，并按照标书中所附的投标文件规格编写，并上传至本项目政采云系统。
EN: 4.4.1 This project requires preparation of the bid documents according to the above contents, written in accordance with the bidding document specifications attached to the bid, and uploaded to the Government Procurement Cloud system for this project.

<!-- id: p000184 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.4.2 投标人应按采购文件的内容与要求和提供的格式编写其投标文件，投标人不得缺少或留空任何采购文件要求填写的表格或提交的资料。如采购文件没有提供格式的，投标人可自行设置。
EN: 4.4.2 The bidder shall prepare its bidding documents according to the contents and requirements of the procurement documents and the provided formats. The bidder shall not omit or leave blank any forms required to be completed or materials required to be submitted by the procurement documents. If the procurement documents do not provide a format, the bidder may set its own.

<!-- id: p000185 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.4.3投标人应将投标文件按一定的顺序编排、并编制目录、逐页标注连续页码，装定成册。
EN: 4.4.3 The bidder shall arrange the bidding documents in a certain order, prepare a table of contents, mark continuous page numbers page by page, and bind them into a volume.

<!-- id: p000186 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5、投标报价
EN: 5. Bid Quotation

<!-- id: p000187 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.1  投标人应在投标明细报价表上标明本次采购拟提供货物的单价和总价。明细报价表标明所有报价均以到达现场（招标文件规定的地点）并安装合格的全部费用，必须包括招标文件中所需设备报价（含税金）、运输费、装卸费、保管、搬运、安装、调试、验收、拆装、培训、备品备件、保险、售后服务、税款、测试、质检、检验、行政许可及相关证书等直至交付采购人正常使用前的一切费用。计算评标总价时，以货物到达招标人指定交货地点为依据。
EN: 5.1 The bidder shall indicate the unit price and total price of the goods to be provided in this procurement in the detailed quotation table. The detailed quotation table shall indicate that all quotations include all expenses for delivery to the site (the location specified in the tender documents) and qualified installation, and must include all expenses up to normal use by the purchaser, including equipment quotations required by the tender documents (including taxes), transportation, loading/unloading, storage, handling, installation, commissioning, acceptance, disassembly/reassembly, training, spare parts, insurance, after-sales service, taxes, testing, quality inspection, examination, administrative permits and related certificates, etc. When calculating the total evaluation price, delivery of the goods to the delivery location designated by the tenderer shall serve as the basis.

<!-- id: p000188 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 如投标文件报价出现前后不一致的，除招标文件另有规定外，按以下规定修正，如果不同意下述修改原则，其投标将被拒绝。
EN: If there are inconsistencies in the quotations in the bidding documents, unless otherwise specified in the tender documents, they shall be corrected in accordance with the following provisions. If the bidder does not agree to the following correction principles, its bid will be rejected.

<!-- id: p000189 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.1.1 投标文件中开标一览表（报价表）内容与投标文件中相应内容不一致的，以开标一览表（报价表）为准；
EN: 5.1.1 If the contents of the bid opening summary table (quotation table) in the bidding documents are inconsistent with the corresponding contents in the bidding documents, the bid opening summary table (quotation table) shall prevail;

<!-- id: p000190 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.1.2 大写金额和小写金额不一致的，以大写金额为准；
EN: 5.1.2 If the amount in words and the amount in figures are inconsistent, the amount in words shall prevail;

<!-- id: p000191 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.1.3 单价金额小数点或者百分比有明显错位的，以开标一览表的总价为准 ，并修改单价；
EN: 5.1.3 If there is an obvious misplacement of the decimal point or percentage in the unit price amount, the total price in the bid opening summary table shall prevail, and the unit price shall be corrected accordingly;

<!-- id: p000192 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.1.4 总价金额与单价汇总金额不一致的，以单价金额计算结果为准。
EN: 5.1.4 If the total price amount is inconsistent with the total of the unit price amounts, the calculation result based on the unit price amounts shall prevail.

<!-- id: p000193 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.1.5 同时出现两种以上不一致的，按前本条顺序修正。修正后的报价经投标人确认后产生约束力，投标人不确认的，其投标无效。
EN: 5.1.5 If two or more inconsistencies occur simultaneously, corrections shall be made in the order above. The corrected quotation shall become binding after being confirmed by the bidder; if the bidder does not confirm, its bid is invalid.

<!-- id: p000194 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.1.6 投标明细报价表必须列清设备是包含明细内容，不得只报出设备总价，否则视为实质性不响应招标文件。
EN: 5.1.6 The detailed quotation table must clearly list the detailed contents of the equipment and shall not quote only a total equipment price; otherwise, it shall be deemed a substantive non-response to the tender documents.

<!-- id: p000195 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.2  投标人如果免费提供某项产品、部件或服务，除在价格栏中填写“0”外，还必须在备注栏中声明免费或赠送。
EN: 5.2 If the bidder provides any product, component, or service free of charge, in addition to entering “0” in the price column, it must also state in the remarks column that it is free or a giveaway.

<!-- id: p000196 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.3  投标报价时应注意下列几点：
EN: 5.3 The following points should be noted when quoting:

<!-- id: p000197 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.3.1 本项目如非因重大需求变化导致成本增加，不得追加费用，投标人应该考虑但没有考虑到的任何费用将由投标人自行承担。
EN: 5.3.1 For this project, unless costs increase due to major changes in requirements, no additional fees may be added. Any expenses that the bidder should have considered but did not consider shall be borne by the bidder.

<!-- id: p000198 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.3.2 投标人应在明细报价表标明所有报价均以到达现场（招标文件规定的地点）并安装合格的全部费用，必须包括招标文件中所需设备报价（含税金）、运输费、装卸费、保管、搬运、安装、调试、验收、拆装、培训、备品备件、保险、售后服务、税款、测试、质检、检验、行政许可及相关证书等直至交付采购人正常使用前的一切费用。
EN: 5.3.2 The bidder shall indicate in the detailed quotation table that all quotations include all expenses for delivery to the site (the location specified in the tender documents) and qualified installation, and must include all expenses up to normal use by the purchaser, including equipment quotations required by the tender documents (including taxes), transportation, loading/unloading, storage, handling, installation, commissioning, acceptance, disassembly/reassembly, training, spare parts, insurance, after-sales service, taxes, testing, quality inspection, examination, administrative permits and related certificates, etc.

<!-- id: p000199 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.3.3 招标文件中特别要求的备品备件、易损件和专用工具的费用。
EN: 5.3.3 Costs of spare parts, consumable parts, and special tools specifically required in the tender documents.

<!-- id: p000200 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.3.4 投标人提供的货物，其货物的投标价即货到交货地点的交货价格，包括制造、组装该货物所使用的零部件及原材料已付的全部关税、销售税和其他税。
EN: 5.3.4 For the goods provided by the bidder, the bid price for the goods is the delivery price when the goods arrive at the delivery location, including all customs duties, sales taxes, and other taxes already paid on the parts and raw materials used to manufacture and assemble the goods.

<!-- id: p000201 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.4  投标人应对投标货物提供完整的详细的书面说明。
EN: 5.4 The bidder shall provide a complete and detailed written description of the bid goods.

<!-- id: p000202 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.5  报价超过最高限价的，该报价为无效报价，不进入商务评比。
EN: 5.5 If the quotation exceeds the maximum price limit, it is an invalid quotation and will not enter the commercial evaluation.

<!-- id: p000203 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.6  评标委员会认为投标人的报价明显低于其他通过符合性审查投标人的报价，有可能影响产品质量或者不能诚信履约的，应当要求该投标人在评标系统合理的时间内提供成本构成说明，必要时提交相关证明材料；投标人不能证明其报价合理性的，评标委员会应当将其作为无效投标处理。
EN: 5.6 If the evaluation committee believes that a bidder’s quotation is significantly lower than the quotations of other bidders who have passed the compliance review, and that it may affect product quality or make it impossible to perform the contract in good faith, it shall require the bidder to provide a cost composition explanation within a reasonable time in the evaluation system and, if necessary, submit relevant supporting materials; if the bidder cannot prove that its quotation is reasonable, the evaluation committee shall treat it as an invalid bid.

<!-- id: p000204 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 6、招标文件规定的技术文件
EN: 6. Technical Documents Required by the Tender Documents

<!-- id: p000205 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 6.1  投标人须提交证明拟供货物和服务符合招标文件规定的文件资料，作为投标文件的一部分。
EN: 6.1 The bidder shall submit documents and materials proving that the goods and services to be supplied conform to the provisions of the tender documents, as part of the bidding documents.

<!-- id: p000206 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 6.2  上述文件可以是文字资料、图纸和数据等，并提供规格、技术参数偏离表。
EN: 6.2 The above documents may be written materials, drawings, data, etc., and a specifications/technical-parameter deviation table shall be provided.

<!-- id: p000207 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 6.3  没有按要求提供资料或提供资料不完全的，将被视为对招标文件没有做出实质性响应，其风险由投标人自行承担。
EN: 6.3 Failure to provide materials as required, or provision of incomplete materials, will be deemed as not making a substantive response to the tender documents, and the risk shall be borne by the bidder.

<!-- id: p000208 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 6.4  投标人提供的设备必须是正规厂家生产的高质量产品，不能提供劣质三无产品（无厂址,无商标,无合格证）。
EN: 6.4 The equipment provided by the bidder must be high-quality products produced by legitimate manufacturers, and may not be inferior “three-no” products (no manufacturer address, no trademark, no certificate of conformity).

<!-- id: p000209 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 7、投标有效期
EN: 7. Bid Validity Period

<!-- id: p000210 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 7.1  投标文件从投标之日起，投标有效期90天。
EN: 7.1 From the date of bidding, the bid validity period is 90 days.

<!-- id: p000211 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 7.2  在特殊情况下，采购方可与投标人协商延长投标文件的有效期。
EN: 7.2 Under special circumstances, the purchaser may consult with the bidder to extend the validity period of the bidding documents.

<!-- id: p000212 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 8、投标文件的签署规定
EN: 8. Signing Requirements for Bidding Documents

<!-- id: p000213 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 8.1  投标文件的页面必须用印刷体打印，提倡双面打印。
EN: 8.1 The pages of the bidding documents must be printed in print font; double-sided printing is encouraged.

<!-- id: p000214 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 8.2  投标文件应清楚工整，一般不准修改。个别非实质性修改之处应由投标人的被授权人或法人代表签章。
EN: 8.2 The bidding documents shall be clear and neat and generally may not be altered. Individual non-substantive modifications shall be signed/sealed by the bidder’s authorized person or legal representative.

<!-- id: p000215 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 8.3  投标文件应由法人代表或授权代表在规定的签章处逐一签署并加盖单位公章。所有投标人签字、法人代表签字、法人代表授权人签字和其它签字处必须加盖具有法律效力的投标人的印章后，投标文件方为有效。
EN: 8.3 The bidding documents shall be signed one by one at the specified signature/seal locations by the legal representative or an authorized representative and affixed with the company’s official seal. The bidding documents are valid only after the bidder’s legally effective seal is affixed at all signature locations, including bidder signatures, legal representative signatures, authorized representative signatures, and other signatures.

<!-- id: p000216 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 8.4  电报、电话、传真、电子邮件等形式的投标概不接受。
EN: 8.4 Bids in the form of telegram, telephone, fax, email, etc. will not be accepted.

<!-- id: p000217 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 9、投标文件的修改和撤销
EN: 9. Amendment and Withdrawal of Bidding Documents

<!-- id: p000218 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 9.1  投标人在递交投标文件后，可在规定的投标截止时间之前，对其投标文件以书面通知的形式进行修改或撤销。该通知须有投标代理人的签字，并得到采购方的确认。
EN: 9.1 After submitting the bidding documents, the bidder may, before the specified bid submission deadline, amend or withdraw its bidding documents by written notice. Such notice must be signed by the bidder’s agent and confirmed by the purchaser.

<!-- id: p000219 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 9.2  投标人对投标文件修改的书面材料或撤消通知应按招标文件要求进行密封、标注和递交，并注明“修改投标文件”或“撤消投标”字样，修改或撤消的内容须按招标文件的要求签署、盖章，并作为投标文件和组成部分。
EN: 9.2 The written materials for amending the bidding documents or the withdrawal notice shall be sealed, marked, and submitted in accordance with the tender document requirements, and shall be marked with “Amendment to Bidding Documents” or “Withdrawal of Bid.” The amended or withdrawn contents shall be signed and sealed in accordance with the tender document requirements, and shall constitute part of the bidding documents.

<!-- id: p000220 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 9.3  对投标文件修改的书面材料应于投标截止日前送达采购方，投标截止时间以后不得修改投标文件。
EN: 9.3 Written materials for amendments to the bidding documents shall be delivered to the purchaser before the bid submission deadline. No amendments to the bidding documents may be made after the deadline.

<!-- id: p000221 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 9.4  投标人不得在开标后至投标有效期满前撤销投标文件，否则采购方将没收其投标保证金。
EN: 9.4 The bidder shall not withdraw its bidding documents after bid opening and before the expiration of the bid validity period; otherwise, the purchaser will forfeit its bid bond.

<!-- id: p000222 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 第三章  投标文件的递交
EN: Chapter 3  Submission of Bidding Documents

<!-- id: p000223 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 10、投标文件的密封和标记
EN: 10. Sealing and Marking of Bidding Documents

<!-- id: p000224 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 10.1  投标人应在投标截止时间之前完成政采云系统中的标书上传步骤。
EN: 10.1 The bidder shall complete the bid document upload steps in the Government Procurement Cloud system before the bid submission deadline.

<!-- id: p000225 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 10.2  发生下列情况之一的投标文件被视为无效：
EN: 10.2 A bidding document shall be deemed invalid if any of the following occurs:

<!-- id: p000226 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （1） 投标截止时间以后上传的投标文件；
EN: (1) Bidding documents uploaded after the bid submission deadline;

<!-- id: p000227 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （2） 与采购文件有重大偏离的投标文件；
EN: (2) Bidding documents that have material deviations from the procurement documents;

<!-- id: p000228 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （3） 投标文件应盖而未盖公章或非本公司公章的、不按正确位置盖章的；未装订、未密封、法定代表人授权书、资格声明函等填写不完整或有涂改未加盖公章的；
EN: (3) Where the bid documents should bear the official seal but do not, or bear a seal that is not the company’s official seal, or the seal is affixed in an incorrect position; where they are not bound, not sealed, or the legal representative’s power of attorney, qualification declaration letter, etc. are incomplete or have alterations without being affixed with the official seal;

<!-- id: p000229 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （4） 无“报价一览表”的投标文件；
EN: (4) Bid documents without a “Bid Price Summary Table”;

<!-- id: p000230 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （5） “报价一览表”没有加盖公章的；
EN: (5) Where the “Bid Price Summary Table” is not affixed with the official seal;

<!-- id: p000231 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （6） 未按规定交纳投标保证金的投标文件；
EN: (6) Bid documents where the bid security is not paid as required;

<!-- id: p000232 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （7） 出现影响采购公正的违法违规行为的投标性文件。
EN: (7) Bidding documents involving illegal or non-compliant acts that affect the fairness of the procurement.

<!-- id: p000233 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 11、投标文件递交截止时间及开标时间和地点
EN: 11. Deadline for submission of bid documents and the time and place of bid opening

<!-- id: p000234 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 11.1  投标文件递交截止时间：2025年7月31日11：00时（北京时间）。投标文件上传至政采云线上平台。
EN: 11.1 Deadline for submission of bid documents: 2025年7月31日11：00时 (Beijing time). Bid documents shall be uploaded to the Zhengcaiyun online platform.

<!-- id: p000235 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 11.2  开标时间：同投标文件递交截止时间。
EN: 11.2 Bid opening time: the same as the deadline for submission of bid documents.

<!-- id: p000236 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 11.3  开标地点：电子评标，不见面开标，新疆政府采购网（http://www.ccgp-xinjiang.gov.cn）政采云线上平台。
EN: 11.3 Place of bid opening: electronic evaluation; no in-person bid opening; the Zhengcaiyun online platform of the Xinjiang Government Procurement Network (http://www.ccgp-xinjiang.gov.cn).

<!-- id: p000237 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 11.4  所有投标文件都必须在采购方规定的投标截止时间之前上传采购文件指定的地点，在此之后上传的投标文件，为无效投标，投标文件将一律被拒绝。
EN: 11.4 All bid documents must be uploaded to the location designated in the procurement documents before the bid deadline specified by the Purchaser. Bid documents uploaded after that time are invalid bids and will be rejected.

<!-- id: p000238 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 11.5  出现因招标文件的修改而推迟投标截止时间的情况时，投标人则须按采购方的书面修改通知重新规定的投标时间递交。
EN: 11.5 Where the bid submission deadline is postponed due to amendments to the bidding documents, bidders shall submit bids at the bid time re-specified in the Purchaser’s written amendment notice.

<!-- id: p000239 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 12、投标保证金
EN: 12. Bid Security

<!-- id: p000240 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 12.1 投标保证金是为了保护采购方免遭因投标人的行为而蒙受损失。采购方在因投标人的行为受到损害时可根据本须知的规定没收投标人的投标保证金。
EN: 12.1 The bid security is to protect the Purchaser from losses arising from the bidder’s conduct. Where the Purchaser suffers damage due to the bidder’s conduct, it may forfeit the bidder’s bid security in accordance with these Instructions.

<!-- id: p000241 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 12.2  投标保证金的货币为人民币，并采用转账、电汇、网银、电子保函等非现金形式交纳，如电汇产生的一切费用由投标人自行承担。
EN: 12.2 The currency of the bid security shall be RMB, and it shall be paid in non-cash forms such as bank transfer, telegraphic transfer, online banking, or electronic guarantee. Any fees arising from telegraphic transfer shall be borne by the bidder.

<!-- id: p000242 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 12.3  投标保证金金额：
EN: 12.3 Amount of bid security:

<!-- id: p000243 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 人民币：叁万柒仟元整（37000.00元）
EN: RMB: thirty-seven thousand yuan only (37000.00元)

<!-- id: p000244 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 12.4  递交投标保证金截止时间：2025年7月31日11：00时（北京时间），凡未提交投标保证金的投标，将视为自动放弃投标，投标将被拒绝。
EN: 12.4 Deadline for submitting the bid security: 2025年7月31日11：00时 (Beijing time). Any bid for which the bid security is not submitted will be deemed an automatic waiver of bidding and will be rejected.

<!-- id: p000245 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 12.5  资格审查时没有提供投标保证金递交证明的投标，将被视为非响应性投标予以拒绝。
EN: 12.5 Bids that do not provide proof of submission of the bid security during qualification review will be deemed non-responsive bids and rejected.

<!-- id: p000246 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 12.6  未中标投标人的保证金, 代理机构将在中标通知书发出后5个工作日内，原额退还投标人（无息）。我公司每周一至周五按原账户退还保证金，如因投标人账户原因无法原账户退还的，请投标人及时与我公司联系。
EN: 12.6 The bid security of unsuccessful bidders: the agency will refund it in full (without interest) to the bidder within 5 working days after issuance of the Notice of Award. Our company refunds the bid security to the original account every Monday to Friday; if it cannot be refunded to the original account due to the bidder’s account reasons, please contact our company promptly.

<!-- id: p000247 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 12.7  中标人的投标保证金在合同签订后5个工作日内退还。
EN: 12.7 The successful bidder’s bid security will be refunded within 5 working days after the contract is signed.

<!-- id: p000248 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 12.8  下列任何情况发生时，投标保证金将不予退还。
EN: 12.8 The bid security will not be refunded in any of the following circumstances.

<!-- id: p000249 type: paragraph -->
ZH: (1)  投标人在提交投标文件截止时间后撤回投标文件的；
EN: (1) The bidder withdraws its bid documents after the deadline for submission of bid documents;

<!-- id: p000250 type: paragraph -->
ZH: (2)  投标人在投标文件中提供虚假材料的；
EN: (2) The bidder provides false materials in the bid documents;

<!-- id: p000251 type: paragraph -->
ZH: (3)  除因不可抗力或招标文件认可的情形外中标投标人不与采购人签订合同的；
EN: (3) Except for force majeure or circumstances recognized by the bidding documents, the successful bidder fails to sign the contract with the Purchaser;

<!-- id: p000252 type: paragraph -->
ZH: (4)  投标人与采购人、其他投标人或者采购代理机构恶意串通的；
EN: (4) The bidder maliciously colludes with the Purchaser, other bidders, or the procurement agency;

<!-- id: p000253 type: paragraph -->
ZH: (5)  本招标文件中或《政府采购货物和服务招标投标管理办法》第七十五条规定的其他不予退还投标保证金的情形。
EN: (5) Other circumstances under which the bid security shall not be refunded as provided in these bidding documents or Article 75 of the Measures for the Administration of Bidding and Tendering for Government Procurement of Goods and Services.

<!-- id: p000254 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 上述不予退还投标保证金的情况并给代理机构造成损失的，还要承担赔偿责任。
EN: Where any of the above non-refund circumstances occur and cause losses to the agency, compensation liability shall also be borne.

<!-- id: p000255 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 第四章  开标
EN: Chapter 4 Bid Opening

<!-- id: p000256 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 13、开标
EN: 13. Bid Opening

<!-- id: p000257 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 13.1  招标代理机构在“投标人须知前列表”中规定的日期、时间和地点组织招标会，邀请所有投标人在线（政采云平台）参加。所有投标人的法定代表人或其授权代表人均应准时在政采云平台签到，并在开启投标文件解密时，30分钟内解密成功，如因投标人自身原因未按规定时间内解密，导致的后果由投标人自行承担；如遇特殊情况未在规定时间解密，经招标人、监督人同意可以将备份投标文件发送至代理公司联系邮箱，由代理公司上传至本项目。投标人少于3家的不得开标，招标人应当重新招标。
EN: 13.1 The tendering agency shall organize the tender meeting on the date, time, and place specified in the “Bidder Instructions – Front Table”, and invite all bidders to participate online (Zhengcaiyun platform). The legal representative of each bidder or its authorized representative shall check in on the Zhengcaiyun platform on time and, when bid document decryption is opened, successfully decrypt within 30 minutes. If a bidder fails to decrypt within the specified time due to its own reasons, the consequences shall be borne by the bidder; if due to special circumstances decryption is not completed within the specified time, with the consent of the tenderer and the supervisor, the backup bid documents may be sent to the agency company’s contact email address, and the agency company will upload them to this project. Where there are fewer than 3 bidders, bids shall not be opened, and the tenderer shall re-tender.

<!-- id: p000258 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 13.2  开标会议由招标代理人组织并主持。解密成功后，各投标人可以查看所有投标人的报价及交货完工期、质保期，如没有异议在开标记录表上在线签字确认。
EN: 13.2 The bid opening meeting shall be organized and chaired by the tendering agent. After successful decryption, each bidder may view all bidders’ quotations as well as the delivery/completion period and warranty period; if there is no objection, sign and confirm online on the bid opening record form.

<!-- id: p000259 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 13.3 不同投标人的投标文件异常一致或者投标报价呈规律性差异的，视为投标人相互串通投标，评标委员会应当否决其投标，招投标监督管理机构依法追究投标人及相关人员责任。
EN: 13.3 Where bid documents of different bidders are abnormally identical or bid quotations show regular differences, this shall be deemed collusive bidding among bidders; the evaluation committee shall reject their bids, and the bid/tender supervision and administration authority shall pursue the responsibility of the bidders and relevant personnel in accordance with law.

<!-- id: p000260 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 14.招标会议程序：
EN: 14. Tender meeting procedure:

<!-- id: p000261 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 14.1  开标一般按照以下程序进行：
EN: 14.1 Bid opening is generally conducted according to the following procedures:

<!-- id: p000262 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 1、在采购文件确定的投标截止时间停止接受投标文件，确认投标人数量是否符合开标要求；
EN: 1. Stop accepting bid documents at the bid submission deadline specified in the procurement documents, and confirm whether the number of bidders meets the requirements for bid opening;

<!-- id: p000263 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2、由招标人在政采云系统依次查验以下内容，并确认查验结果：
EN: 2. The tenderer shall, in the Zhengcaiyun system, check the following contents in sequence and confirm the inspection results:

<!-- id: p000264 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （1）提供有效的营业执照等证明材料（加盖单位公章）；
EN: (1) Provide valid business license and other supporting materials (affixed with the entity’s official seal);

<!-- id: p000265 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （2）提供 2023 年度或 2024 年度的会计报表或审计报告，包括资产负债表、利润表、现金流量表和财务情况说明书，复印件加盖公章。(成立不足 1 年的提供自成立以来的财务审计报告或财务报表)；
EN: (2) Provide the 2023年度 or 2024年度 accounting statements or audit report, including the balance sheet, income statement, cash flow statement, and financial statement notes/explanatory statement, with copies affixed with the official seal. (If established for less than 1 year, provide the financial audit report or financial statements since establishment);

<!-- id: p000266 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （3）根据项目需求提供履行合同所必需的设备和专业技术能力加盖公章的声明；
EN: (3) Provide, according to project needs, a statement (affixed with official seal) of the equipment and professional technical capability necessary to perform the contract;

<!-- id: p000267 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （4）提供近期 3 个月完税证明和近期 3 个月社会保险的凭据证明 材料复印件加盖公章；如依法免税或不需要缴纳社会保障资金的，应提供相应文件证明；
EN: (4) Provide copies (affixed with official seal) of tax payment certificates for the most recent 3 months and vouchers/certificates for social insurance for the most recent 3 months; if exempt from tax or not required to pay social security funds according to law, provide corresponding documentary proof;

<!-- id: p000268 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （5）提供参加本次政府采购活动前3年内在经营活动中没有重大违法记录声明函（加盖公章）；
EN: (5) Provide a declaration letter (affixed with official seal) that there have been no major illegal records in business operations within the 3 years prior to participating in this government procurement activity;

<!-- id: p000269 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （6）法人授权委托书或法人身份证明书，授权人或法人（法人参与投标时提供）有效身份证明；
EN: (6) Power of attorney for legal person authorization or certificate of the legal representative’s identity, and valid identification of the authorized person or the legal representative (provided when the legal representative participates in bidding);

<!-- id: p000270 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （7）提供承诺函：单位负责人为同一人或者存在直接控股、管理关系的不同投标人，未参加同一合同项下的政府采购活动；
EN: (7) Provide a letter of commitment: different bidders whose person in charge is the same person or that have direct controlling-shareholding or management relationships have not participated in government procurement activities under the same contract;

<!-- id: p000271 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （8）投标保证金交纳凭证；
EN: (8) Proof of payment of the bid security;

<!-- id: p000272 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 注：不能上传以上营业执照及证书的，可上传法定有效的公证件。资格审查不合格或不能提供保证金证明时，将取消其投标资格。
EN: Note: If the above business license and certificates cannot be uploaded, legally valid notarized documents may be uploaded. Where the qualification review is unqualified or proof of the bid security cannot be provided, its bidding qualification will be cancelled.

<!-- id: p000273 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 3、招标人在资格审查表上签名确认；
EN: 3. The tenderer signs to confirm on the qualification review form;

<!-- id: p000274 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4、资格审查环节结束，进行后续评标。
EN: 4. After the qualification review stage ends, proceed with subsequent bid evaluation.

<!-- id: p000275 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 14.2  有下列情形之一的，监督人应当场宣布投标无效：
EN: 14.2 Where any of the following circumstances occurs, the supervisor shall announce on the spot that the bid is invalid:

<!-- id: p000276 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 1、投标人资质审查未通过的；
EN: 1. The bidder fails the qualification review;

<!-- id: p000277 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2、投标保证金提交不符合规定的；
EN: 2. Submission of the bid security does not comply with requirements;

<!-- id: p000278 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 3、投标总报价高于招标控制价（即最高投标限价）的。
EN: 3. The total bid quotation is higher than the tender control price (i.e., the maximum bid limit).

<!-- id: p000279 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 第五章  定标
EN: Chapter 5 Award (Determination of the Winning Bid)

<!-- id: p000280 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 15、定标标准
EN: 15. Award Criteria

<!-- id: p000281 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 15.1   由评审小组采用综合评分法对投标人的投标文件和报价进行综合评分。综合评分法，是指投标文件满足招标文件全部实质性要求，且按评审因素的量化指标评审得分最高的投标人为中标候选投标人的评审方法。
EN: 15.1 The evaluation panel shall use the comprehensive scoring method to comprehensively score bidders’ bid documents and quotations. The comprehensive scoring method refers to the evaluation method in which the bid documents meet all substantive requirements of the bidding documents, and the bidder with the highest score according to the quantified indicators of the evaluation factors is the winning-candidate bidder.

<!-- id: p000282 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 价格分应当采用低价优先法计算，即满足招标文件要求且投标价格最低的投标报价为评标基准价，其价格分为满分 。其他投标人的价格分统一下列公式计算：
EN: The price score shall be calculated using the low-price-first method, i.e., the lowest bid quotation that meets the requirements of the bidding documents is the evaluation benchmark price, and its price score is the full score. The price scores of other bidders are calculated uniformly using the following formula:

<!-- id: p000283 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 投标报价得分=（评标基准价/投标报价）*100%*价格分值
EN: Bid quotation score = (evaluation benchmark price / bid quotation) * 100% * price score value

<!-- id: p000284 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 评标总得分=F1*A1+F2*A2+……Fn*AN
EN: Total evaluation score = F1*A1 + F2*A2 + ……Fn*AN

<!-- id: p000285 type: paragraph -->
ZH: F1、F2……Fn分别为各项评审因素的得分；A1、A2……An分别为各项评审因素所占的权重（A1+A2+……+An=1）。
EN: F1, F2……Fn are the scores of each evaluation factor; A1, A2……An are the weights of each evaluation factor (A1+A2+……+An=1).

<!-- id: p000286 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 评标过程中，不得去掉报价中的最高报价和最低报价。
EN: During bid evaluation, the highest quotation and the lowest quotation in the quotations shall not be removed.

<!-- id: p000287 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 评审小组根据依据此原则按由高到低排序向采购人推荐3家投标中标候选人,或拒绝所有投标人，采购人根据专家推荐意见与建议，确定和公布最终中标单位。
EN: Based on this principle, the evaluation panel ranks from high to low and recommends 3 bidders as winning candidates to the Purchaser, or rejects all bidders; the Purchaser, based on the experts’ recommendations and suggestions, determines and announces the final winning contractor.

<!-- id: p000288 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 15.2  原则上应将排名第一的投标人确定为中标投标人，若有以下情形之一者也可确定推荐排名第二的投标人为中标人：
EN: 15.2 In principle, the first-ranked bidder shall be determined as the successful bidder; if any of the following circumstances occurs, the recommended second-ranked bidder may also be determined as the successful bidder:

<!-- id: p000289 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 15.2.1 排名第一的中标候选人放弃中标；
EN: 15.2.1 The first-ranked winning candidate waives the award;

<!-- id: p000290 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 15.2.2 排名第一的中标候选人因不可抗力提出不能履行合同。
EN: 15.2.2 The first-ranked winning candidate states it cannot perform the contract due to force majeure.

<!-- id: p000291 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 15.2.3 在接到中标通知30日内第一中标排序人未能如期签订合同。如果第二中标排序人不能满足此条要求（满足其他中标条件），采购人选择与中标排名第三的中标候选人进行技术、商务评审。
EN: 15.2.3 Within 30 days of receiving the Notice of Award, the first-ranked candidate fails to sign the contract as scheduled. If the second-ranked candidate cannot meet this requirement (while meeting other award conditions), the Purchaser will choose to conduct technical and commercial evaluation with the third-ranked winning candidate.

<!-- id: p000292 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 15.3  评审组无义务向投标人进行任何有关招标、评审的解释工作。
EN: 15.3 The evaluation panel has no obligation to provide bidders with any explanations relating to tendering or evaluation.

<!-- id: p000293 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 15.4  在确定和公布最终中标中标人前，采购人认为必要时，可以对认为有必要了解或核实的问题进行考查、核实。
EN: 15.4 Before determining and announcing the final successful bidder, the Purchaser may, when deemed necessary, investigate and verify matters it considers necessary to understand or verify.

<!-- id: p000294 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 15.5  如果确定该投标人无条件圆满履行合同，评审小组将对下一个可能中标的投标人资格做出类似的审查。
EN: 15.5 If it is determined that the bidder will unconditionally and satisfactorily perform the contract, the evaluation panel will conduct a similar review of the qualifications of the next potential winning bidder.

<!-- id: p000295 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 16. 结果公示
EN: 16. Public Notice of Results

<!-- id: p000296 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 依法必须进行招标的项目，招标人在新疆政府采购网公示中标候选人。公示内容包括：采购人及其委托的采购代理机构的名称、地址、联系方式，项目名称和项目编号，中标人名称、地址和中标金额，主要中标标的的名称、规格型号、数量、单价、服务要求，中标公告期限以及评审专家名单。
EN: For projects that must be tendered in accordance with law, the tenderer shall publish the winning candidates on the Xinjiang Government Procurement Network. The published content includes: the name, address, and contact information of the Purchaser and the procurement agency it entrusts; the project name and project number; the successful bidder’s name, address, and winning amount; the name, specification/model, quantity, unit price, and service requirements of the main winning subject matter; the duration of the award announcement; and the list of evaluation experts.

<!-- id: p000297 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 17、中标通知书
EN: 17. Notice of Award

<!-- id: p000298 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 发结果公示的同时向第一中标候选人发出《中标通知书》，《中标通知书》将作为签订合同的依据。
EN: At the same time as issuing the results public notice, issue the “Notice of Award” to the first winning candidate; the “Notice of Award” will serve as the basis for signing the contract.

<!-- id: p000299 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 第六章  授予合同
EN: Chapter 6 Contract Award

<!-- id: p000300 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 18、签订合同
EN: 18. Signing the Contract

<!-- id: p000301 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 18.1  中标方收到采购方的《中标通知书》后30日内，按照招标文件的约定和中标人投标文件中的承诺与采购单位签订书面合同，所签订的合同不得对招标文件和中标人的投标文件作实质性修改。
EN: 18.1 Within 30 days after the successful party receives the Purchaser’s “Notice of Award”, it shall sign a written contract with the purchasing unit in accordance with the stipulations of the bidding documents and the commitments in the successful bidder’s bid documents. The signed contract shall not make substantive modifications to the bidding documents or the successful bidder’s bid documents.

<!-- id: p000302 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 18.2  采购方在授予合同时，有权对招标文件中规定的货物和服务的数量在10%的幅度内予以增加或减少。但不得对单价更改。
EN: 18.2 When awarding the contract, the Purchaser has the right to increase or decrease the quantities of goods and services specified in the bidding documents within a range of 10%. However, the unit price shall not be changed.

<!-- id: p000303 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 18.3  如中标方拒签合同，则按违约处理。采购方没收其投标保证金。
EN: 18.3 If the successful party refuses to sign the contract, it shall be handled as a breach. The Purchaser will forfeit its bid security.

<!-- id: p000304 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 18.4  招标文件、中标人投标文件及其澄清文件等，均为签订经济合同的依据。
EN: 18.4 The bidding documents, the successful bidder’s bid documents and its clarification documents, etc. are all the basis for signing the economic contract.

<!-- id: p000305 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 第七章 质疑
EN: Chapter 7 Challenges (Objections)

<!-- id: p000306 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 19、质疑
EN: 19. Challenges (Objections)

<!-- id: p000307 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 19.1  采购程序受《中华人民共和国政府采购法》、《政府采购法实施条例》《政府采购货物和服务招标投标管理办法》（财政部第87号令）和相关法律法规的约束，并受到严格的内部监督，以确保授予合同过程的公平、公正。
EN: 19.1 The procurement procedures are governed by the PRC Government Procurement Law, the Implementing Regulations of the Government Procurement Law, the Measures for the Administration of Bidding and Tendering for Government Procurement of Goods and Services (财政部第87号令), and relevant laws and regulations, and are subject to strict internal supervision to ensure fairness and impartiality in the contract award process.

<!-- id: p000308 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 19.2  投标人已经参与了投标，并于开标后对招标文件提出质疑的，其质疑应当被视为无效质疑。
EN: 19.2 If a bidder has already participated in bidding and raises an objection to the bidding documents after bid opening, such objection shall be deemed an invalid objection.

<!-- id: p000309 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 19.3  投标人对开标过程有异议的，应当在开标现场提出，由监督组及招标人、招标代理机构作出答复或更正，对开标过程未提出质疑的，在开标程序结束后或招标工作结束后，其对开标过程的质疑视为无效。
EN: 19.3 If a bidder has objections to the bid opening process, it shall raise them at the bid opening site, and the supervision group and the tenderer and tendering agency shall respond or make corrections. If no objection is raised to the bid opening process, after the bid opening procedure ends or after the tendering work ends, any objection to the bid opening process shall be deemed invalid.

<!-- id: p000310 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 19.4  投标人认为中标结果使自己的权益受到损害的，可以在知道或者应知其权益受到损害之日起七个工作日内，以书面形式向代理机构提出质疑。
EN: 19.4 If a bidder believes that the award result has harmed its rights and interests, it may, within seven working days from the date it knew or should have known that its rights and interests were harmed, raise a written objection to the agency.

<!-- id: p000311 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 19.5  质疑应严格按照招标程序以质疑函书面格式向代理机构提出，质疑函须经法定代表人签字并加盖公章。
EN: 19.5 Objections shall be submitted to the agency in strict accordance with the tendering procedures in the written format of an objection letter. The objection letter must be signed by the legal representative and affixed with the official seal.

<!-- id: p000312 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 19.6  按照“谁主张、谁举证”的原则，质疑时应当提供相关证明材料。质疑材料按照一式二份提供。
EN: 19.6 In accordance with the principle of “whoever asserts, bears the burden of proof”, supporting evidence materials shall be provided when raising an objection. Objection materials shall be provided in two copies.

<!-- id: p000313 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 19.7  有下列情形之一的，属于无效质疑，代理机构可不予受理：
EN: 19.7 Any of the following circumstances constitutes an invalid objection, and the agency may refuse to accept it:

<!-- id: p000314 type: paragraph -->
ZH: A 未在有效期限内提出质疑的；
EN: A Objection not raised within the valid time limit;

<!-- id: p000315 type: paragraph -->
ZH: B 质疑未以书面形式提出的；
EN: B Objection not raised in written form;

<!-- id: p000316 type: paragraph -->
ZH: C 质疑函没有法定代表人签署并加盖单位公章的；
EN: C The objection letter is not signed by the legal representative and not affixed with the entity’s official seal;

<!-- id: p000317 type: paragraph -->
ZH: D 质疑事项已经进入投诉或者诉讼程序的；
EN: D The objection matter has already entered complaint or litigation procedures;

<!-- id: p000318 type: paragraph -->
ZH: E 其它不符合受理条件的情形。
EN: E Other circumstances that do not meet the acceptance conditions.

<!-- id: p000319 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 19.8  代理机构将在收到书面质疑后7个工作日内作出答复或相关处理决定，并以书面形式通知质疑投标企业和其他有关部门。
EN: 19.8 The agency will, within 7 working days after receiving the written objection, make a reply or relevant handling decision, and notify the objecting bidding enterprise and other relevant departments in writing.

<!-- id: p000320 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 19.9  投标人进行虚假和恶意质疑的，代理机构可以提请行业行政监管部门将其列入不良记录名单，在一至三年内禁止参加本地区招投标活动，并将处理决定在相关媒体上公布。
EN: 19.9 If a bidder raises false or malicious objections, the agency may request the industry administrative regulatory authority to place it on the list of bad records, prohibit it from participating in bidding activities in this region for one to three years, and publish the handling decision in relevant media.

<!-- id: p000321 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 19.10 投标人对代理机构的答复不满意以及代理机构未在规定的时间内做出答复的，可以在答复期满后15个工作日内向行业行政监管部门进行投诉。
EN: 19.10 If the bidder is dissatisfied with the agency’s reply or the agency fails to reply within the specified time, it may lodge a complaint with the industry administrative regulatory authority within 15 working days after the reply period expires.

<!-- id: p000322 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 第四部分  采购货物清单及技术规格要求
EN: Part IV List of Procured Goods and Technical Specification Requirements

<!-- id: p000323 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 一、项目内容
EN: I. Project Content

<!-- id: p000324 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 项目名称：新疆警察学院网络空间安全综合实验室建设项目（三次）
EN: Project name: Xinjiang Police College Cyberspace Security Comprehensive Laboratory Construction Project (三次)

<!-- id: p000325 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 采购预算：370万元
EN: Procurement budget: 370万元

<!-- id: p000326 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 二、项目介绍
EN: II. Project Introduction

<!-- id: p000327 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 新疆警察学院信息工程系承担着“网络安全与执法”及“网络空间安全”两个本科专业的课程教学，根据专业的人才培养目标，以提升学生在网络安全领域的实践创新能力和未来职业发展能力为导向，突出学生需掌握的行业产业或者职业领域的扎实基础理论、系统专门知识，以及解决实际问题的能力，拟建设网络空间安全综合实验室，以便于学生在实验实践、综合实训、第二课堂、创新创业、技能竞赛等环节与国内知名网络安全企业充分合作，建立长期的产教融合培养机制。
EN: The Information Engineering Department of Xinjiang Police College undertakes course teaching for the two undergraduate majors “网络安全与执法” and “网络空间安全”. In accordance with the majors’ talent training objectives, and guided by improving students’ practical innovation capability and future career development capability in the cybersecurity field, it emphasizes the solid foundational theory, systematic specialized knowledge, and practical problem-solving ability that students need to master in the relevant industry or occupational field. It plans to build a Cyberspace Security Comprehensive Laboratory so that students can fully cooperate with well-known domestic cybersecurity enterprises in experimental practice, comprehensive practical training, the Second Classroom, innovation and entrepreneurship, skills competitions, and other links, establishing a long-term industry-education integration training mechanism.

<!-- id: p000328 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 项目需建设一套虚拟化、实战化教学实践环境，主要包括网络空间安全教学平台及相关精品实践教学课程、实战教学信息资源库，网络攻防平台含赛题及攻防培训服务，AI一体化平台及课程，服务器、学生电脑等基础软硬件设备，并对四间实训室进行装修改造。项目建设完成后应能够支撑两个专业现行人才培养方案中的网络安全相关课程的配套实验；能够支撑综合实训、第二课堂等2-3周的集中实践课程；能够支撑10周的专业实习或其他大型场景式的项目综合实践；能够基于平台开展网络安全竞赛及网络对抗、攻防演练等活动。通过理论授课、案例研讨、实验操作、模拟对抗、比赛竞技等多个方面的实践活动提高师生的攻防对抗实战能力，同时可增加实践渠道、丰富培养途径，激励越来越多的学生积极参与，从而提升专业核心竞争力。
EN: The project needs to build a virtualized, combat-oriented teaching practice environment, mainly including a Cyberspace Security teaching platform and related high-quality practice teaching courses, a practical teaching information resource repository, an attack-defense platform including competition problems and attack-defense training services, an AI integrated platform and courses, foundational software and hardware equipment such as servers and student computers, and renovation and remodeling of four training rooms. After completion, the project should be able to support the accompanying experiments for cybersecurity-related courses in the current talent training programs of the two majors; support 2-3 weeks of集中 practice courses such as comprehensive practical training and the Second Classroom; support 10 weeks of professional internship or other large-scale scenario-based project comprehensive practice; and carry out cybersecurity competitions, cyber confrontation, and attack-defense drills based on the platform. Through practical activities in multiple aspects such as theoretical lectures, case discussions, experimental operations, simulated confrontation, and competitive contests, it improves the practical attack-defense confrontation capability of teachers and students, while also increasing practice channels and enriching training pathways, motivating more and more students to actively participate, thereby enhancing the major’s core competitiveness.

<!-- id: p000329 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 三、技术规格、参数与要求
EN: III. Technical Specifications, Parameters, and Requirements

<!-- id: p000330 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 注：技术参数中标▲项需提供相关证明材料，且下一级条款无论是否加注“▲”标志仍为标▲项。标“#项且加    ”项需提供现场功能演示。
EN: Note: For technical parameters, ▲-marked items must provide relevant supporting materials, and sub-clauses at the next level are ▲-marked items regardless of whether they are marked with “▲”. Items marked “#项且加    ” must provide on-site function demonstrations.

<!-- id: t000043 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: | 序号 | 设备名称 | 技术参数 | 单位 | 数量 | 中小企 业划分 标准所 属行业 |
EN_ROW: | No. | Equipment Name | Technical Parameters | Unit | Quantity | Industry under SME classification standard |

<!-- id: t000044 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: | 1 | 网络空间安全教学平台 | （一）教学平台管理及性能要求 | 套 | 1 | 软件和信息技术服务业 |
EN_ROW: | 1 | Cyberspace Security Teaching Platform | (I) Teaching platform management and performance requirements | set | 1 | Software and information technology services |

<!-- id: t000045 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: |  |  | 1、系统采用B/S架构设计，兼容多种浏览器。可提供多层次互动仿真实验环境，支持学生通过一系列的单项、综合类型实验完成网络空间安全及网络安全与执法两个专业的实验实践课程教学支撑。 |  |  |  |
EN_ROW: |  |  | 1. The system adopts a B/S architecture design and is compatible with multiple browsers. It can provide multi-level interactive simulated experiment environments, supporting students to complete teaching support for experimental/practical courses for the two majors, Cyberspace Security and Cybersecurity and Law Enforcement, through a series of single-item and comprehensive experiments. |  |  |  |

<!-- id: t000046 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: |  |  | 2、提供可视化图形界面，直观展示系统资源。支持对人员、任务、场景的统计，可展示资源负载情况及系统资源使用率。 |  |  |  |
EN_ROW: |  |  | 2. Provide a visual graphical interface to intuitively display system resources. Support statistics on personnel, tasks, and scenarios, and display resource load conditions and system resource utilization. |  |  |  |

<!-- id: t000047 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: |  |  | ▲3、教师能够对知识体系进行系统化管理，按照课程体系、课程、章、单元、小节等进行多级课程结构的管理，支持新增、修改、删除、查询、导入、导出等常规操作。 |  |  |  |
EN_ROW: |  |  | ▲3. Teachers can systematically manage the knowledge system, managing multi-level course structures by curriculum system, course, chapter, unit, section, etc., and supporting routine operations such as add, modify, delete, query, import, and export. |  |  |  |

<!-- id: t000048 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: |  |  | ▲4、教师能够自行创建实验场景，构建过程各步骤能够独立保存，后续可继当前暂存状态继续编辑。可通过图形化、拖拽式网络拓扑绘制进行任务场景设计，可对场景拓扑中的各个节点对应的资源模板进行绑定，支持构建各类具有安全策略的多安全区仿真实验场景。需提供一份场景设计方案样例。 |  |  |  |
EN_ROW: |  |  | ▲4. Teachers can create experiment scenarios on their own; each step of the building process can be saved independently, and later editing can continue from the current saved state. Task scenarios can be designed via graphical, drag-and-drop network topology drawing; resource templates corresponding to each node in the scenario topology can be bound, supporting construction of various multi-security-zone simulated experiment scenarios with security policies. A sample scene design方案 shall be provided. |  |  |  |

<!-- id: t000049 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: |  |  | 5、支持学生对学习的课程进行评价和留言，教师角色可以查看，并对留言进行回复。 |  |  |  |
EN_ROW: |  |  | 5. Support students to evaluate and leave messages on courses they study; teachers can view and reply to messages. |  |  |  |

<!-- id: t000050 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: |  |  | 6、 支持系统中现存的主机、网络、虚拟机、模板、路由器、防火墙等资源的统计信息的展示。 |  |  |  |
EN_ROW: |  |  | 6. Support displaying statistical information for existing resources in the system such as hosts, networks, virtual machines, templates, routers, firewalls, etc. |  |  |  |

<!-- id: t000051 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: |  |  | 7、支持计算资源负载，系统能够按照负载策略将虚拟机或镜像分配到不同的计算引擎服务器运行。 |  |  |  |
EN_ROW: |  |  | 7. Support compute resource load; the system can allocate virtual machines or images to run on different compute engine servers according to load policies. |  |  |  |

<!-- id: t000052 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: |  |  | 8、支持网络资源隔离管理，利用网络子网隔离技术将不同的虚拟网络进行隔离，用以降低模拟场景的流量和网络的复杂性，同时保障虚拟机资源之间的通信互不干扰及安全性等。 |  |  |  |
EN_ROW: |  |  | 8. Support network resource isolation management; use subnet isolation technology to isolate different virtual networks, reducing traffic and network complexity of simulated scenarios while ensuring non-interference and security of communications among virtual machine resources. |  |  |  |

<!-- id: t000053 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: |  |  | 9、支持存储资源负载，系统能够按照负载策略将虚拟机或镜像分配到不同的存储节点服务器运行。 |  |  |  |
EN_ROW: |  |  | 9. Support storage resource load; the system can allocate virtual machines or images to run on different storage node servers according to load policies. |  |  |  |

<!-- id: t000054 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: |  |  | 10、新建学习任务时，支持老师将教学任务进行批量下发，以避免重复工作量。 |  |  |  |
EN_ROW: |  |  | 10. When creating new learning tasks, support teachers to batch-assign teaching tasks to avoid repetitive workload. |  |  |  |

<!-- id: t000055 type: table_row -->

<!-- id: t000062 type: table_row -->

<!-- id: t000063 type: table_row -->

EN_ROW: |  |  | (III) Teaching platform target resource requirements |  |  |  |

<!-- id: t000064 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: |  |  | 1、平台需提供教学培训课程，需保障交付时能够完全支持专业培养方案中实验实践课程教学，后续在质保期内按季度进行更新，确保课程与时俱进。 |  |  |  |
EN_ROW: |  |  | 1. The platform shall provide teaching/training courses, ensuring that upon delivery it can fully support teaching of experimental/practical courses in the major training program; thereafter, it shall be updated quarterly during the warranty period to keep the courses up to date. |  |  |  |

<!-- id: t000065 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: |  |  | 2、平台需提供题库资源，支持单选题、多选题、判断题、填空题等多种类型。 |  |  |  |
EN_ROW: |  |  | 2. The platform shall provide a question bank, supporting multiple types such as single-choice, multiple-choice, true/false, and fill-in-the-blank questions. |  |  |  |

<!-- id: t000066 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: |  |  | 3、平台应内置操作系统、应用服务及公共漏洞靶标，支持的靶机操作系统类型应包含Windows、Linux等，需提供多种安全设备虚拟靶标。 |  |  |  |
EN_ROW: |  |  | 3. The platform shall have built-in operating systems, application services, and public-vulnerability targets; supported target-machine OS types shall include Windows, Linux, etc., and multiple virtual targets for security devices shall be provided. |  |  |  |

<!-- id: t000067 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: | 2 | 网络空间安全教学精品课程 | 针对网络空间安全专业及网络安全与执法专业的培养方案，提供以下与教学计划匹配的实验资源支持： | 套 | 1 | 软件和信息技术服务业 |
EN_ROW: | 2 | High-quality Cyberspace Security Teaching Courses | For the training programs of the Cyberspace Security major and the Cybersecurity and Law Enforcement major, provide the following experimental resource support matching the teaching plan: | set | 1 | Software and information technology services |

<!-- id: t000068 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: |  |  | 1、网络安全基础实验课，需支持防火墙、入侵检测等基础实验支持。 |  |  |  |
EN_ROW: |  |  | 1. Basic cybersecurity lab course: shall support basic labs such as firewall and intrusion detection. |  |  |  |

<!-- id: t000069 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: |  |  | 2、密码学及应用实验课，需提供分组密码、序列密码、流密码等实验支持。 |  |  |  |
EN_ROW: |  |  | 2. Cryptography and applications lab course: shall provide lab support for block ciphers, sequence ciphers, stream ciphers, etc. |  |  |  |

<!-- id: t000070 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: |  |  | 3、操作系统安全实验课，需提供操作系统安全及操作系统安全评测等实验支持。 |  |  |  |
EN_ROW: |  |  | 3. Operating system security lab course: shall provide lab support for operating system security and operating system security evaluation, etc. |  |  |  |

<!-- id: t000071 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: |  |  | 4、Web安全实验课，需提供SQL注入型漏洞、跨站脚本攻击漏洞等通用web框架漏洞及web代码审计等实验支持。 |  |  |  |
EN_ROW: |  |  | 4. Web security lab course: shall provide lab support for common web framework vulnerabilities such as SQL injection vulnerabilities and cross-site scripting vulnerabilities, as well as web code auditing, etc. |  |  |  |

<!-- id: t000072 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: |  |  | 5、网络攻防技术实验课，需提供攻击技术方向及防御技术方向的实验支持。 |  |  |  |
EN_ROW: |  |  | 5. Network attack-and-defense technology lab course: shall provide lab support for the attack-technique track and the defense-technique track. |  |  |  |

<!-- id: t000073 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: |  |  | 6、网络对抗技术实验课，需提供对抗环境搭建、攻击路径规划与实施、防守方防御策略部署、应急响应等实验支持。 |  |  |  |
EN_ROW: |  |  | 6. Network confrontation technology lab course: shall provide lab support for building confrontation environments, attack-path planning and implementation, defender-side defense strategy deployment, incident response, etc. |  |  |  |

<!-- id: t000074 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: |  |  | 7、网络安全协议分析实验课，需提供网络安全协议分析实验支持。 |  |  |  |
EN_ROW: |  |  | 7. Cybersecurity protocol analysis lab course: shall provide lab support for cybersecurity protocol analysis. |  |  |  |

<!-- id: t000075 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: |  |  | 8、软件安全与逆向分析实验课，需提供代码审计、反汇编、反调试技术等实验支持。 |  |  |  |
EN_ROW: |  |  | 8. Software security and reverse analysis lab course: shall provide lab support for code auditing, disassembly, anti-debugging techniques, etc. |  |  |  |

<!-- id: t000076 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: |  |  | 9、电子数据取证分析技术实验课，需提供操作系统取证、病毒取证、网络流量数据包取证等实验支持。 |  |  |  |
EN_ROW: |  |  | 9. Electronic data forensics analysis technology lab course: shall provide lab support for operating system forensics, malware/virus forensics, and network traffic packet forensics, etc. |  |  |  |

<!-- id: t000077 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: |  |  | 10、网络情报获取与分析技术实验课，需提供情报收集、流量分析等实验支持。 |  |  |  |

ZH_ROW: | 26 | 附属配套集成服务 | 包含4间实验室附属配套集成建设：<br/>1、采用非屏蔽六类网线，全面涵盖布线作业，同时配备所需电线，并包含施工费。<br/>2、施工期间对旧实验室造成破损的修复工作，将对顶面、墙面、地面受损区域，开展针对性修复，具体面积现场约定，最终实施面积以现场勘察实际尺寸为主。<br/>（包含：墙面：破损墙面找平、墙面粉刷修复；顶面：顶面防尘修复、顶面龙骨框架修复和吊装；<br/>地面：地面防尘修复、接地导线、等电位端子箱、接地铜排、地板下静电泄露网、防静电地板、踢脚线；其他修复：钢化玻璃隔断、窗户封堵、房间原隔墙拆除、房间原破损防静电地板拆除、修复工作完成后，及时清运因修复产生的垃圾 ，确保场地恢复整洁。）<br/>3、培训服务：为了配合学校更好的使用实验平台，需中标方对提供的设备进行现场培训服务，直到相关专业老师、学生可熟练使用平台。培训目的： 熟练使用平台及所涉及的配套设备。除基础软件操作培训外，需为重点管理员提供高级运维培训（如故障处理、数据备份等）。要求供应商提供完整的操作手册及应急处理指南。培训人员：相关专业教师及学生。培训目的：保障前期实验平台使用中所发生的设备问题及技术保障。<br/>4、试用期现场技术服务：提供1名以上的技术人员在实验平台试用期间进行现场服务，试用期时间1 个月。<br/>5、投标人需包含软件平台对接学校统一身份认证系统/教务系统，定期维护和更新的所有费用。<br/>6、因后期涉及整体校区地理位置变迁，投标人需包含整体项目迁移造成的所有费用。含（不仅限于）：设备迁移、系统部署、综合布线及其他应考虑的费用。 | 项 | 1 | 软件和信息技术服务业 |
EN_ROW: | 26 | Ancillary supporting integrated services | Includes ancillary supporting integrated construction for 4 laboratories:<br/>1. Use unshielded Category 6 network cables to fully cover cabling work, and also provide the required power cables, including construction labor costs.<br/>2. Repair work for damage to old laboratories during construction: for damaged areas of ceilings, walls, and floors, carry out targeted repairs; the specific area shall be agreed on-site, and the final implemented area shall be based on actual dimensions from on-site survey.<br/>（Includes: walls: leveling of damaged wall surfaces, repainting/repair; ceilings: dust-proof repair, ceiling keel/frame repair and hoisting;<br/>floors: dust-proof repair, grounding conductors, equipotential terminal boxes, grounding copper busbars, electrostatic leakage mesh under the floor, anti-static flooring, skirting boards; other repairs: tempered-glass partitions, window sealing, demolition of original room partitions, demolition of original damaged anti-static flooring in rooms; after repairs are completed, promptly remove and dispose of garbage generated by the repairs to ensure the site is restored to cleanliness.）<br/>3. Training services: to support the school’s better use of the laboratory platform, the winning bidder must provide on-site training services for the provided equipment until relevant professional teachers and students can proficiently use the platform. Training objective: proficient use of the platform and the supporting equipment involved. In addition to basic software operation training, advanced O&M training (e.g., troubleshooting, data backup, etc.) must be provided for key administrators. The supplier is required to provide a complete operation manual and emergency handling guide. Trainees: relevant professional teachers and students. Training objective: ensure resolution of equipment issues and technical support encountered in early-stage use of the laboratory platform.<br/>4. On-site technical service during the trial period: provide at least 1 technician to provide on-site service during the laboratory platform trial period; trial period is 1 month.<br/>5. The bidder must include all costs for the software platform to integrate with the school’s unified identity authentication system/academic affairs system, and for regular maintenance and updates.<br/>6. As the overall campus geographic location may change later, the bidder must include all costs caused by overall project migration, including (but not limited to): equipment relocation, system deployment, integrated cabling, and other costs that should be considered. | item | 1 | Software and information technology services |

<!-- id: p000331 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 四、服务要求
EN: IV. Service Requirements

<!-- id: p000332 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 交付时间及服务期：
EN: Delivery time and service period:

<!-- id: p000333 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 供货方应在合同签订后三个月内完成实训室装修改造，并将货物送至甲方指定地点，相关的运输费、保险、保管、货物灭失及损毁风险在交付前由供货方承担。
EN: The supplier shall complete the renovation and retrofit of the training room within three months after the contract is signed and deliver the goods to the location designated by Party A; the related transportation costs, insurance, storage, and the risks of loss and damage to the goods prior to delivery shall be borne by the supplier.

<!-- id: p000334 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 设备安装、调试达到技术要求规定的指标并正常运行5个工作日后，进行采购方指定人员培训，培训完成后双方指定人员对照技术指标进行验证验收测试，签署交付测试报告。
EN: After the equipment is installed and commissioned to meet the indicators specified in the technical requirements and runs normally for 5 working days, training shall be provided for personnel designated by the purchaser; after training, designated personnel of both parties shall conduct verification acceptance testing against the technical indicators and sign the delivery test report.

<!-- id: p000335 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 在交付测试通过后5个工作日内采购方组织交付专家评审会，完成并验收合格交付使用。
EN: Within 5 working days after the delivery test is passed, the purchaser shall organize an expert delivery review meeting; upon completion and passing acceptance, it shall be delivered for use.

<!-- id: p000336 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 质保及免费服务期：从验收合格之日起三年。
EN: Warranty and free service period: three years from the date of acceptance.

<!-- id: p000337 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 服务要求：
EN: Service requirements:

<!-- id: p000338 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 提供7×24小时免费网站支持服务、电话支持服务、邮件支持服务、远程协助服务。接到采购人通知2小时内给予明确答复，6小时内到达现场维修。维修人员到现场后若问题特殊无法现场修复的，供货方需在24小时内给出合理解决方案。
EN: Provide 7×24-hour free website support, telephone support, email support, and remote assistance services. Provide a clear response within 2 hours of receiving the purchaser’s notice and arrive on site for maintenance within 6 hours. If, after maintenance personnel arrive on site, the issue is special and cannot be repaired on site, the supplier shall provide a reasonable solution within 24 hours.

<!-- id: p000339 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 软件产品升级服务：提供3年的软件产品升级服务，包括但不限于系统软件的升级和补丁、课程、题库等教学资源包和竞赛环境的升级服务。
EN: Software product upgrade service: provide 3 years of software product upgrade services, including but not limited to upgrades and patches for system software, and upgrade services for teaching resource packages such as courses and question banks, as well as competition environments.

<!-- id: p000340 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 提供正式验收交付之日起原厂3年免费硬件软件售后服务，至少包括：硬件维保、产品性能调优服务、产品故障排除服务、代码缺陷修复服务、产品操作使用方面的技术咨询服务；
EN: From the date of official acceptance and delivery, provide the original manufacturer’s 3-year free hardware and software after-sales service, including at least: hardware maintenance, product performance tuning services, product troubleshooting services, code defect repair services, and technical consulting services on product operation and use;

<!-- id: p000341 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 服务团队指定专门的接口人，每年至少2次巡检服务。
EN: The service team shall designate a dedicated point of contact and provide at least 2 inspection visits per year.

<!-- id: p000342 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 针对以上售后服务要求，供应商需在投标文件中提供书面承诺函，并加盖公章。
EN: For the above after-sales service requirements, the supplier shall provide a written commitment letter in the bidding documents and affix its official seal.

<!-- id: p000351 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 使 用 说 明
EN: Instructions for Use

<!-- id: p000352 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 1.本合同标准文本适用于购买现成货物的采购项目，不包括需要供应商定制开发、创新研发的货物采购项目。
EN: 1. This standard contract text applies to procurement projects for purchasing off-the-shelf goods and does not include goods procurement projects requiring supplier-customized development or innovative R&D.

<!-- id: p000353 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2.本合同标准文本为政府采购货物买卖合同编制提供参考，可以结合采购项目具体情况，对文本作必要的调整修订后使用。
EN: 2. This standard contract text provides a reference for preparing government procurement goods sale and purchase contracts; it may be used after making necessary adjustments and revisions in light of the specific circumstances of the procurement project.

<!-- id: p000354 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 3.本合同标准文本各条款中，如涉及填写多家供应商、制造商，多种采购标的、分包主要内容等信息的，可根据采购项目具体情况添加信息项。
EN: 3. In the clauses of this standard contract text, where information such as multiple suppliers/manufacturers, multiple procurement items, or main subcontract content needs to be filled in, information fields may be added according to the specific circumstances of the procurement project.

ZH: 分期付款：  （应明确分期支付合同款项的各期比例和支付条件，各期支付条件应与分期履约验收情况挂钩） ，其中涉及预付款的： （应明确预付款的支付比例和支付条件）
EN: Installment payment:  (the proportion and payment conditions of each installment shall be specified, and the payment conditions of each installment shall be linked to staged performance acceptance) where prepayment is involved: (the prepayment proportion and payment conditions shall be specified)

<!-- id: p000424 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 成本补偿：      （应明确按照成本补偿方式的支付方式和支付条件）
EN: Cost reimbursement:      (the payment method and payment conditions under the cost reimbursement method shall be specified)

<!-- id: p000425 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 绩效激励：      （应明确按照绩效激励方式的支付方式和支付条件）
EN: Performance incentive:      (the payment method and payment conditions under the performance incentive method shall be specified)

<!-- id: p000426 type: paragraph -->

EN: Contract performance

<!-- id: p000427 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （1）起始日期：    年   月   日，完成日期：    年   月   日。
EN: (1) Start date:    year   month   day, completion date:    year   month   day.

EN: (2) Place of performance:

EN: (3) Performance security: whether to collect a performance bond: Yes    No

EN: (5) Contents of performance acceptance: (should include the performance of each technical and commercial requirement, especially implementation of policies such as government procurement support for SMEs, support for green development, and rural revitalization)

ZH: 本协议书与下列文件一起构成合同文件，如下述文件之间有任何抵触、矛盾或歧义，应按以下顺序解释：
EN: This agreement, together with the following documents, constitutes the contract documents. If there is any conflict, contradiction, or ambiguity among the following documents, they shall be interpreted in the following order:

<!-- id: p000456 type: paragraph -->
