<!-- id: p000471 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 第二节 政府采购合同通用条款
EN: Section 2  General Terms of the Government Procurement Contract

<!-- id: p000472 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 1. 定义
EN: 1. Definitions

<!-- id: p000473 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 1.1合同当事人
EN: 1.1 Contract parties

<!-- id: p000474 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （1）采购人（以下称甲方）是指使用财政性资金，通过政府采购方式向供应商购买货物及其相关服务的国家机关、事业单位、团体组织。
EN: (1) The purchaser (hereinafter “Party A”) refers to state organs, public institutions, or social organizations that use fiscal funds to purchase goods and related services from suppliers through government procurement.

<!-- id: p000475 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （2）供应商（以下称乙方）是指参加政府采购活动并且中标（成交），向采购人提供合同约定的货物及其相关服务的法人、非法人组织或者自然人。
EN: (2) The supplier (hereinafter “Party B”) refers to a legal person, unincorporated organization, or natural person that participates in government procurement activities and is awarded (transacted), and provides the purchaser with the goods and related services agreed in the contract.

<!-- id: p000476 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （3）其他合同主体是指除采购人和供应商以外，依法参与合同缔结或履行，享有权利、承担义务的合同当事人。
EN: (3) Other contract subjects refer to contract parties other than the purchaser and supplier that, in accordance with law, participate in contract conclusion or performance and enjoy rights and assume obligations.

<!-- id: p000477 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 1.2本合同下列术语应解释为：
EN: 1.2 The following terms in this contract shall be interpreted as:

<!-- id: p000478 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （1）“合同”系指合同当事人意思表示达成一致的任何协议，包括签署的政府采购合同协议书及其变更、补充协议，政府采购合同专用条款，政府采购合同通用条款，中标（成交）通知书，投标（响应）文件，采购文件，有关技术文件和图纸，以及国家法律、行政法规和规章制度规定或合同约定的作为合同组成部分的其他文件。
EN: (1) “Contract” refers to any agreement in which the contract parties’ expressions of intent are consistent, including the signed government procurement contract agreement and its amendments and supplementary agreements, the special terms of the government procurement contract, the general terms of the government procurement contract, the notice of award (transaction), the bidding (response) documents, the procurement documents, relevant technical documents and drawings, and other documents stipulated by national laws, administrative regulations, and rules, or agreed in the contract, as part of the contract.

<!-- id: p000479 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （2）“合同价款”系指根据本合同规定乙方在全面履行合同义务后甲方应支付给乙方的价款。
EN: (2) “Contract price” refers to the price payable by Party A to Party B after Party B fully performs its contractual obligations under this contract.

<!-- id: p000480 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （3）“货物”系指乙方根据本合同规定须向甲方提供的各种形态和种类的物品，包括原材料、设备、产品（包括软件）及相关的其备品备件、工具、手册及其他技术资料和材料等。
EN: (3) “Goods” refer to items of various forms and types that Party B must provide to Party A under this contract, including raw materials, equipment, products (including software), and related spare parts, tools, manuals, and other technical documents and materials.

<!-- id: p000481 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （4）“相关服务”系指根据合同规定，乙方应提供的与货物有关的技术、管理和其他服务，包括但不限于：管理和质量保证、运输、保险、检验、现场准备、安装、集成、调试、培训、维修、废弃处置、技术支持等以及合同中规定乙方应承担的其他义务。
EN: (4) “Related services” refer to technical, management, and other services related to the goods that Party B shall provide under the contract, including but not limited to: management and quality assurance, transportation, insurance, inspection, site preparation, installation, integration, commissioning, training, repair, disposal, technical support, and other obligations Party B shall undertake as stipulated in the contract.

<!-- id: p000482 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （5）“分包”系指中标（成交）供应商按采购文件、投标（响应）文件的规定，根据分包意向协议，将中标（成交）项目中的部分履约内容，分给具有相应资质条件的供应商履行合同的行为。
EN: (5) “Subcontracting” refers to the act whereby the awarded (transacted) supplier, in accordance with the procurement documents and bidding (response) documents and based on the subcontracting intention agreement, subcontracts part of the performance content of the awarded (transacted) project to suppliers with corresponding qualifications to perform the contract.

<!-- id: p000483 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （6）“联合体”系指由两个以上的自然人、法人或者非法人组织组成，以一个供应商的身份共同参加政府采购的主体。联合体各方应在签订合同协议书前向甲方提交联合协议，且明确牵头人及各成员单位的工作分工、权利、义务、责任，联合体各方应共同与甲方签订合同，就合同约定的事项对甲方承担连带责任。联合体具体要求见【政府采购合同专用条款】。
EN: (6) “Consortium” refers to a joint entity composed of two or more natural persons, legal persons, or unincorporated organizations that jointly participate in government procurement as one supplier. Before signing the contract agreement, all parties of the consortium shall submit the consortium agreement to Party A and specify the lead party, division of work, rights, obligations, and responsibilities of each member unit. All consortium parties shall jointly sign the contract with Party A and bear joint and several liability to Party A for matters agreed in the contract. Specific requirements for a consortium are set out in 【Special Terms of the Government Procurement Contract】.

<!-- id: p000484 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （7）其他术语解释，见【政府采购合同专用条款】。
EN: (7) For other term explanations, see 【Special Terms of the Government Procurement Contract】.

<!-- id: p000485 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 合同标的及金额
EN: Contract subject matter and amount

<!-- id: p000486 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2.1 合同标的及金额应与中标（成交）结果一致。乙方为履行本合同而发生的所有费用均应包含在合同价款中，甲方不再另行支付其他任何费用。
EN: 2.1 The contract subject matter and amount shall be consistent with the awarded (transacted) result. All costs incurred by Party B for performing this contract shall be included in the contract price, and Party A shall not pay any other expenses separately.

<!-- id: p000487 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 3. 履行合同的时间、地点和方式
EN: 3. Time, place, and manner of contract performance

<!-- id: p000488 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 3.1 乙方应当在约定的时间、地点，按照约定方式履行合同。
EN: 3.1 Party B shall perform the contract at the agreed time and place and in the agreed manner.

<!-- id: p000489 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4. 甲方的权利和义务
EN: 4. Rights and obligations of Party A

<!-- id: p000490 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.1 签署合同后，甲方应确定项目负责人（或项目联系人），负责与本合同有关的事务。甲方有权对乙方的履约行为进行检查，并及时确认乙方提交的事项。甲方应当配合乙方完成相关项目实施工作。
EN: 4.1 After signing the contract, Party A shall designate a project leader (or project contact person) responsible for matters related to this contract. Party A has the right to inspect Party B’s performance and promptly confirm matters submitted by Party B. Party A shall cooperate with Party B in completing the implementation of relevant project work.

<!-- id: p000491 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.2 甲方有权要求乙方按时提交各阶段有关安排计划，并有权定期核对乙方提供货物数量、规格、质量等内容。甲方有权督促乙方工作并要求乙方更换不符合要求的货物。
EN: 4.2 Party A has the right to require Party B to submit schedule/arrangement plans for each stage on time, and has the right to periodically verify the quantities, specifications, quality, etc. of the goods provided by Party B. Party A has the right to supervise Party B’s work and require Party B to replace goods that do not meet requirements.

<!-- id: p000492 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.3 甲方有权要求乙方对缺陷部分予以修复，并按合同约定享有货物保修及其他合同约定的权利。
EN: 4.3 Party A has the right to require Party B to repair defective parts and, in accordance with the contract, enjoy the goods warranty and other rights agreed in the contract.

<!-- id: p000493 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.4 甲方应当按照合同约定及时对交付的货物进行验收，未在【政府采购合同专用条款】约定的期限内对乙方履约提出任何异议或者向乙方作出任何说明的，视为验收通过。
EN: 4.4 Party A shall accept the delivered goods in a timely manner in accordance with the contract. If Party A does not raise any objection to Party B’s performance or provide any explanation to Party B within the time limit agreed in 【Special Terms of the Government Procurement Contract】, acceptance shall be deemed passed.

<!-- id: p000494 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.5 甲方应当根据合同约定及时向乙方支付合同价款，不得以内部人员变更、履行内部付款流程等为由，拒绝或迟延支付。
EN: 4.5 Party A shall pay the contract price to Party B in a timely manner in accordance with the contract and shall not refuse or delay payment on the grounds of internal personnel changes, internal payment procedures, etc.

<!-- id: p000495 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.6 国家法律法规规定及【政府采购合同专用条款】约定应由甲方承担的其他义务和责任。
EN: 4.6 Other obligations and responsibilities that shall be borne by Party A as stipulated by national laws and regulations and agreed in 【Special Terms of the Government Procurement Contract】.

<!-- id: p000496 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5. 乙方的权利和义务
EN: 5. Rights and obligations of Party B

<!-- id: p000497 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.1 签署合同后，乙方应确定项目负责人（或项目联系人），负责与本合同有关的事务。
EN: 5.1 After signing the contract, Party B shall designate a project leader (or project contact person) responsible for matters related to this contract.

<!-- id: p000498 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.2 乙方应按照合同要求履约，充分合理安排，确保提供的货物及相关服务符合合同有关要求。接受项目行业管理部门及政府有关部门的指导，配合甲方的履约检查及验收，并负责项目实施过程中的所有协调工作。
EN: 5.2 Party B shall perform as required by the contract, make full and reasonable arrangements, and ensure that the goods and related services provided meet the contract requirements. Party B shall accept guidance from the project’s industry management department and relevant government departments, cooperate with Party A’s performance inspections and acceptance, and be responsible for all coordination work during project implementation.

<!-- id: p000499 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.3乙方有权根据合同约定向甲方收取合同价款。
EN: 5.3 Party B has the right to collect the contract price from Party A in accordance with the contract.

<!-- id: p000500 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.4国家法律法规规定及【政府采购合同专用条款】约定应由乙方承担的其他义务和责任。
EN: 5.4 Other obligations and responsibilities that shall be borne by Party B as stipulated by national laws and regulations and agreed in 【Special Terms of the Government Procurement Contract】.

<!-- id: p000501 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 合同履行
EN: Contract performance

<!-- id: p000502 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 6.1 甲乙双方应当按照【政府采购合同专用条款】约定顺序履行合同义务；如果没有先后顺序的，应当同时履行。
EN: 6.1 Party A and Party B shall perform contractual obligations in the order agreed in 【Special Terms of the Government Procurement Contract】; if there is no order, they shall perform simultaneously.

<!-- id: p000503 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 6.2 甲乙双方按照合同约定顺序履行合同义务时，应当先履行一方未履行的，后履行一方有权拒绝其履行请求。先履行一方履行不符合约定的，后履行一方有权拒绝其相应的履行请求。
EN: 6.2 Where Party A and Party B perform contractual obligations in the order agreed in the contract, if the party that should perform first fails to perform, the party that should perform later has the right to refuse its request for performance. If the party that performs first performs in a manner not in conformity with the agreement, the party that performs later has the right to refuse the corresponding request for performance.

<!-- id: p000504 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 7. 货物包装、运输、保险和交付要求
EN: 7. Requirements for packaging, transportation, insurance, and delivery of goods

<!-- id: p000505 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 7.1 本合同涉及商品包装、快递包装的，除【政府采购合同专用条款】另有约定外，包装应适应远距离运输、防潮、防震、防锈和防野蛮装卸等要求，确保货物安全无损地运抵【政府采购合同专用条款】约定的指定现场。
EN: 7.1 Where this contract involves commodity packaging and express packaging, unless otherwise agreed in 【Special Terms of the Government Procurement Contract】, packaging shall meet requirements such as long-distance transportation, moisture-proofing, shock-proofing, rust-proofing, and preventing rough loading/unloading, to ensure the goods arrive safely and intact at the designated site agreed in 【Special Terms of the Government Procurement Contract】.

<!-- id: p000506 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 7.2 除【政府采购合同专用条款】另有约定外，乙方负责办理将货物运抵本合同规定的交货地点，并装卸、交付至甲方的一切运输事项，相关费用应包含在合同价款中。
EN: 7.2 Unless otherwise agreed in 【Special Terms of the Government Procurement Contract】, Party B is responsible for all transportation matters for delivering the goods to the delivery location specified in this contract, including loading/unloading and delivery to Party A; related costs shall be included in the contract price.

<!-- id: p000507 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 7.3 货物保险要求按【政府采购合同专用条款】规定执行。
EN: 7.3 Goods insurance requirements shall be implemented in accordance with 【Special Terms of the Government Procurement Contract】.

<!-- id: p000508 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 7.4 除采购活动对商品包装、快递包装达成具体约定外，乙方提供产品及相关快递服务涉及到具体包装要求的，应不低于《商品包装政府采购需求标准（试行）》《快递包装政府采购需求标准（试行）》标准，并作为履约验收的内容，必要时甲方可以要求乙方在履约验收环节出具检测报告。
EN: 7.4 Except where the procurement activity has reached specific agreements on commodity packaging and express packaging, where Party B’s products and related express services involve specific packaging requirements, such requirements shall be no lower than the standards of the “Government Procurement Demand Standards for Commodity Packaging (Trial)” and the “Government Procurement Demand Standards for Express Packaging (Trial),” and shall be included in performance acceptance. Where necessary, Party A may require Party B to provide an inspection report during the performance acceptance stage.

<!-- id: p000509 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 7.5 乙方在运输到达之前应提前通知甲方，并提示货物运输装卸的注意事项，甲方配合乙方做好货物的接收工作。
EN: 7.5 Party B shall notify Party A in advance before transportation arrives and remind Party A of precautions for loading/unloading during transportation; Party A shall cooperate with Party B in receiving the goods.

<!-- id: p000510 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 7.6 如因包装、运输问题导致货物损毁、丢失或者品质下降，甲方有权要求降价、换货、拒收部分或整批货物，由此产生的费用和损失，均由乙方承担。
EN: 7.6 If the goods are damaged, lost, or experience a quality decline due to packaging or transportation issues, Party A has the right to request a price reduction, replacement, or rejection of part or the entire batch of goods; all resulting costs and losses shall be borne by Party B.

<!-- id: p000511 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 8. 质量标准和保证
EN: 8. Quality standards and warranty

<!-- id: p000512 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 8.1 质量标准
EN: 8.1 Quality standards

<!-- id: p000513 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （1）本合同下提供的货物应符合合同约定的品牌、规格型号、技术性能、配置、质量、数量等要求。质量要求不明确的，按照强制性国家标准履行；没有强制性国家标准的，按照推荐性国家标准履行；没有推荐性国家标准的，按照行业标准履行；没有国家标准、行业标准的，按照通常标准或者符合合同目的的特定标准履行。
EN: (1) The goods provided under this contract shall meet the contract’s agreed requirements for brand, specification/model, technical performance, configuration, quality, quantity, etc. Where quality requirements are unclear, performance shall follow mandatory national standards; where there are no mandatory national standards, performance shall follow recommended national standards; where there are no recommended national standards, performance shall follow industry standards; where there are neither national standards nor industry standards, performance shall follow customary standards or specific standards that meet the purpose of the contract.

<!-- id: p000514 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （2）采用中华人民共和国法定计量单位。
EN: (2) The statutory units of measurement of the People’s Republic of China shall be used.

<!-- id: p000515 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （3）乙方所提供的货物应符合国家有关安全、环保、卫生的规定。
EN: (3) The goods provided by Party B shall comply with national regulations on safety, environmental protection, and hygiene.

<!-- id: p000516 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （4）乙方应向甲方提交所提供货物的技术文件，包括相应的中文技术文件，如：产品目录、图纸、操作手册、使用说明、维护手册或服务指南等。上述文件应包装好随货物一同发运。
EN: (4) Party B shall submit to Party A the technical documents for the goods provided, including corresponding Chinese technical documents, such as product catalogs, drawings, operation manuals, instructions for use, maintenance manuals, or service guides, etc. The above documents shall be properly packaged and shipped together with the goods.

<!-- id: p000517 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 8.2 保证
EN: 8.2 Warranty

<!-- id: p000518 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （1）乙方应保证提供的货物完全符合合同规定的质量、规格和性能要求。乙方应保证货物在正确安装、正常使用和保养条件下，在其使用寿命期内具备合同约定的性能。存在质量保证期的，货物最终交付验收合格后在【政府采购合同专用条款】规定或乙方书面承诺（两者以较长的为准）的质量保证期内，本保证保持有效。
EN: (1) Party B shall guarantee that the goods provided fully meet the quality, specification, and performance requirements stipulated in the contract. Party B shall guarantee that, under correct installation, normal use, and maintenance conditions, the goods possess the performance agreed in the contract throughout their service life. Where a warranty period exists, after final delivery and acceptance of the goods, this warranty remains valid during the warranty period specified in 【Special Terms of the Government Procurement Contract】 or in Party B’s written commitment (whichever is longer).

<!-- id: p000519 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （2）在质量保证期内所发现的缺陷，甲方应尽快以书面形式通知乙方。
EN: (2) For defects discovered during the warranty period, Party A shall notify Party B in writing as soon as possible.

<!-- id: p000520 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （3）乙方收到通知后，应在【政府采购合同专用条款】规定的响应时间内以合理的速度免费维修或更换有缺陷的货物或部件。
EN: (3) After receiving the notice, Party B shall, within the response time specified in 【Special Terms of the Government Procurement Contract】, repair or replace defective goods or parts free of charge at a reasonable speed.

<!-- id: p000521 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （4）在质量保证期内，如果货物的质量或规格与合同不符，或证实货物是有缺陷的，包括潜在的缺陷或使用不符合要求的材料等，甲方可以根据本合同第15.1条规定以书面形式追究乙方的违约责任。
EN: (4) During the warranty period, if the quality or specifications of the goods do not conform to the contract, or if the goods are proven to be defective, including latent defects or use of materials not meeting requirements, Party A may pursue Party B’s liability for breach in writing in accordance with Article 15.1 of this contract.

<!-- id: p000522 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （5）乙方在约定的时间内未能弥补缺陷，甲方可采取必要的补救措施，但其风险和费用将由乙方承担，甲方根据合同约定对乙方行使的其他权利不受影响。
EN: (5) If Party B fails to remedy defects within the agreed time, Party A may take necessary remedial measures, but the risks and expenses shall be borne by Party B; Party A’s other rights exercised against Party B under the contract shall not be affected.

<!-- id: p000523 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 9. 权利瑕疵担保
EN: 9. Warranty against defects of title

<!-- id: p000524 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 9.1 乙方保证对其出售的货物享有合法的权利。
EN: 9.1 Party B warrants that it has lawful rights to the goods it sells.

<!-- id: p000525 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 9.2 乙方保证在交付的货物上不存在抵押权等担保物权。
EN: 9.2 Party B warrants that there are no security interests such as mortgages on the delivered goods.

<!-- id: p000526 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 9.3 如甲方使用上述货物构成对第三人侵权的，则由乙方承担全部责任。
EN: 9.3 If Party A’s use of the above goods constitutes infringement against a third party, Party B shall bear full responsibility.

<!-- id: p000527 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 10. 知识产权保护
EN: 10. Intellectual property protection

<!-- id: p000528 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 10.1 乙方对其所销售的货物应当享有知识产权或经权利人合法授权，保证没有侵犯任何第三人的知识产权等权利。因违反前述约定对第三人构成侵权的，应当由乙方向第三人承担法律责任；甲方依法向第三人赔偿后，有权向乙方追偿。甲方有其他损失的，乙方应当赔偿。
EN: 10.1 Party B shall own the intellectual property rights to the goods it sells or be lawfully authorized by the right holder, and shall ensure that it does not infringe any third party’s rights such as intellectual property rights. If, due to violation of the foregoing, infringement against a third party is constituted, Party B shall bear legal liability to the third party; after Party A compensates the third party in accordance with law, Party A has the right to seek recourse from Party B. If Party A suffers other losses, Party B shall compensate.

<!-- id: p000529 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 11. 保密义务
EN: 11. Confidentiality obligations

<!-- id: p000530 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 11.1 甲、乙双方对采购和合同履行过程中所获悉的国家秘密、工作秘密、商业秘密或者其他应当保密的信息，均有保密义务且不受合同有效期所限，直至该信息成为公开信息。泄露、不正当地使用国家秘密、工作秘密、商业秘密或者其他应当保密的信息，应当承担相应责任。其他应当保密的信息由双方在【政府采购合同专用条款】中约定。
EN: 11.1 Both Party A and Party B have confidentiality obligations for state secrets, work secrets, trade secrets, or other information that should be kept confidential learned during procurement and contract performance, and such obligations are not limited by the validity period of the contract and continue until such information becomes public. Leakage or improper use of state secrets, work secrets, trade secrets, or other confidential information shall bear corresponding responsibilities. Other confidential information shall be agreed by both parties in 【Special Terms of the Government Procurement Contract】.

<!-- id: p000531 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 12. 合同价款支付
EN: 12. Payment of contract price

<!-- id: p000532 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 12.1 合同价款支付按照国库集中支付制度及财政管理相关规定执行。
EN: 12.1 Payment of the contract price shall be implemented in accordance with the treasury centralized payment system and relevant fiscal management provisions.

<!-- id: p000533 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 12.2 对于满足合同约定支付条件的，甲方原则上应当自收到发票后10个工作日内将资金支付到合同约定的乙方账户，不得以机构变动、人员更替、政策调整等为由迟延付款，不得将采购文件和合同中未规定的义务作为向乙方付款的条件。具体合同价款支付时间在【政府采购合同专用条款】中约定。
EN: 12.2 Where the payment conditions agreed in the contract are met, Party A shall, in principle, pay the funds into Party B’s account agreed in the contract within 10 working days after receiving the invoice, and shall not delay payment on the grounds of organizational changes, personnel changes, policy adjustments, etc.; Party A shall not take obligations not stipulated in the procurement documents and the contract as conditions for paying Party B. The specific payment time of the contract price shall be agreed in 【Special Terms of the Government Procurement Contract】.

<!-- id: p000534 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 13. 履约保证金
EN: 13. Performance bond

<!-- id: p000535 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 13.1 乙方应当以支票、汇票、本票或者金融机构、担保机构出具的保函等非现金形式提交。
EN: 13.1 Party B shall submit it in non-cash forms such as checks, drafts, promissory notes, or guarantees issued by financial institutions or guaranty institutions.

<!-- id: p000536 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 13.2 如果乙方出现【政府采购合同专用条款】约定情形的，履约保证金不予退还；如果乙方未能按合同约定全面履行义务，甲方有权从履约保证金中取得补偿或赔偿，且不影响甲方要求乙方承担合同约定的超过履约保证金的违约责任的权利。
EN: 13.2 If Party B falls under circumstances agreed in 【Special Terms of the Government Procurement Contract】, the performance bond shall not be refunded; if Party B fails to fully perform its obligations as agreed in the contract, Party A has the right to obtain compensation or indemnification from the performance bond, without affecting Party A’s right to require Party B to bear breach liabilities exceeding the performance bond as agreed in the contract.

<!-- id: p000537 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 13.3 甲方在项目通过验收后按照【政府采购合同专用条款】规定的时间内将履约保证金退还乙方；逾期退还的，乙方可要求甲方支付违约金，违约金按照【政府采购合同专用条款】规定支付。
EN: 13.3 After the project passes acceptance, Party A shall refund the performance bond to Party B within the time specified in 【Special Terms of the Government Procurement Contract】; if the refund is overdue, Party B may require Party A to pay liquidated damages, which shall be paid in accordance with 【Special Terms of the Government Procurement Contract】.

<!-- id: p000538 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 14. 售后服务
EN: 14. After-sales service

<!-- id: p000539 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 14.1 除项目不涉及或采购活动中明确约定无须承担外，乙方还应提供下列服务：
EN: 14.1 Unless the project does not involve them or it is explicitly agreed in the procurement activity that they need not be undertaken, Party B shall also provide the following services:

<!-- id: p000540 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （1）货物的现场移动、安装、调试、启动监督及技术支持；
EN: (1) On-site relocation, installation, commissioning, start-up supervision, and technical support for the goods;

<!-- id: p000541 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （2）提供货物组装和维修所需的专用工具和辅助材料；
EN: (2) Provide special tools and auxiliary materials required for assembly and repair of the goods;

<!-- id: p000542 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （3）在【政府采购合同专用条款】约定的期限内对所有的货物实施运行监督、维修，但前提条件是该服务并不能免除乙方在质量保证期内所承担的义务；
EN: (3) Implement operation supervision and maintenance for all goods within the period agreed in 【Special Terms of the Government Procurement Contract】, provided that such services do not exempt Party B from its obligations during the warranty period;

<!-- id: p000543 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （4）在制造商所在地或指定现场就货物的安装、启动、运营、维护、废弃处置等对甲方操作人员进行培训；
EN: (4) Train Party A’s operators at the manufacturer’s location or a designated site on installation, start-up, operation, maintenance, disposal, etc. of the goods;

<!-- id: p000544 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （5）依照法律、行政法规的规定或者按照【政府采购合同专用条款】约定，货物在有效使用年限届满后应予回收的，乙方负有自行或者委托第三人对货物予以回收的义务；
EN: (5) In accordance with laws and administrative regulations or as agreed in 【Special Terms of the Government Procurement Contract】, where the goods should be recycled upon expiration of their effective service life, Party B has the obligation to recycle the goods by itself or entrust a third party to do so;

<!-- id: p000545 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （6）【政府采购合同专用条款】规定由乙方提供的其他服务。
EN: (6) Other services to be provided by Party B as stipulated in 【Special Terms of the Government Procurement Contract】.

<!-- id: p000546 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 14.2 乙方提供的售后服务的费用已包含在合同价款中，甲方不再另行支付。
EN: 14.2 The costs of after-sales services provided by Party B are included in the contract price, and Party A shall not pay separately.

<!-- id: p000547 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 15. 违约责任
EN: 15. Liability for breach

<!-- id: p000548 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 15.1质量瑕疵的违约责任
EN: 15.1 Liability for breach due to quality defects

<!-- id: p000549 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 乙方提供的产品不符合合同约定的质量标准或存在产品质量缺陷，甲方有权要求乙方根据【政府采购合同专用条款】要求及时修理、重作、更换，并承担由此给甲方造成的损失。
EN: If Party B’s products do not meet the quality standards agreed in the contract or have product quality defects, Party A has the right to require Party B to promptly repair, remake, or replace them in accordance with 【Special Terms of the Government Procurement Contract】, and Party B shall bear losses caused to Party A thereby.

<!-- id: p000550 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 15.2 迟延交货的违约责任
EN: 15.2 Liability for breach due to delayed delivery

<!-- id: p000551 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （1）乙方应按照本合同规定的时间、地点交货和提供相关服务。在履行合同过程中，如果乙方遇到可能影响按时交货和提供服务的情形时，应及时以书面形式将迟延的事实、可能迟延的期限和理由通知甲方。甲方在收到乙方通知后，应尽快对情况进行评价，并确定是否同意延长交货时间或延期提供服务。
EN: (1) Party B shall deliver the goods and provide related services at the time and place specified in this contract. During contract performance, if Party B encounters circumstances that may affect timely delivery and service provision, it shall promptly notify Party A in writing of the fact of delay, the possible period of delay, and the reasons. After receiving Party B’s notice, Party A shall evaluate the situation as soon as possible and determine whether to agree to extend the delivery time or postpone service provision.

<!-- id: p000552 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （2）如果乙方没有按照合同规定的时间交货和提供相关服务，甲方有权从货款中扣除误期赔偿费而不影响合同项下的其他补救方法，赔偿费按【政府采购合同专用条款】规定执行。如果涉及公共利益，且赔偿金额无法弥补公共利益损失，甲方可要求继续履行或者采取其他补救措施。
EN: (2) If Party B fails to deliver the goods and provide related services at the time specified in the contract, Party A has the right to deduct liquidated damages for delay from the payment for goods without affecting other remedies under the contract; the compensation shall be implemented in accordance with 【Special Terms of the Government Procurement Contract】. If public interests are involved and the compensation amount cannot make up for the loss of public interests, Party A may require continued performance or take other remedial measures.

<!-- id: p000553 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 15.3 迟延支付的违约责任
EN: 15.3 Liability for breach due to delayed payment

<!-- id: p000554 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 甲方存在迟延支付乙方合同款项的，应当承担【政府采购合同专用条款】规定的逾期付款利息。
EN: If Party A delays payment of the contract price to Party B, it shall bear overdue payment interest as stipulated in 【Special Terms of the Government Procurement Contract】.

<!-- id: p000555 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 15.4其他违约责任根据项目实际需要按【政府采购合同专用条款】规定执行。
EN: 15.4 Other breach liabilities shall be implemented in accordance with 【Special Terms of the Government Procurement Contract】 based on actual project needs.

<!-- id: p000556 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 合同变更、中止与终止
EN: Amendment, suspension, and termination of the contract

<!-- id: p000557 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 16.1合同的变更
EN: 16.1 Amendment of the contract

<!-- id: p000558 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 政府采购合同履行中，在不改变合同其他条款的前提下，甲方可以在合同价款10%的范围内追加与合同标的相同的货物，并就此与乙方协商一致后签订补充协议。
EN: During performance of the government procurement contract, without changing other contract terms, Party A may add goods identical to the contract subject matter within 10% of the contract price, and sign a supplementary agreement with Party B after reaching consensus.

<!-- id: p000559 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 16.2合同的中止
EN: 16.2 Suspension of the contract

<!-- id: p000560 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （1）合同履行过程中因供应商就采购文件、采购过程或结果提起投诉的，甲方认为有必要的，可以中止合同的履行。
EN: (1) During contract performance, where a supplier files a complaint regarding the procurement documents, the procurement process, or the results, Party A may suspend contract performance if it deems it necessary.

<!-- id: p000561 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （2）合同履行过程中，如果乙方出现以下情形之一的：1．经营状况严重恶化；2．转移财产、抽逃资金，以逃避债务；3．丧失商业信誉；4．有丧失或者可能丧失履约能力的其他情形，乙方有义务及时告知甲方。甲方有权以书面形式通知乙方中止合同并要求乙方在合理期限内消除相关情形或者提供适当担保。乙方提供适当担保的，合同继续履行；乙方在合理期限内未恢复履约能力且未提供适当担保的，视为拒绝继续履约，甲方有权解除合同并要求乙方承担由此给甲方造成的损失。
EN: (2) During contract performance, if Party B has any of the following circumstances: 1. operating conditions seriously deteriorate; 2. transferring property or withdrawing funds to evade debts; 3. losing business reputation; 4. other circumstances where performance capability is lost or may be lost, Party B has the obligation to promptly inform Party A. Party A has the right to notify Party B in writing to suspend the contract and require Party B to eliminate the relevant circumstances within a reasonable period or provide appropriate security. If Party B provides appropriate security, the contract shall continue to be performed; if Party B fails to restore performance capability within a reasonable period and fails to provide appropriate security, it shall be deemed a refusal to continue performance, and Party A has the right to terminate the contract and require Party B to bear losses caused to Party A thereby.

<!-- id: p000562 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （3）乙方分立、合并或者变更住所的，应当及时以书面形式告知甲方。乙方没有及时告知甲方，致使合同履行发生困难的，甲方可以中止合同履行并要求乙方承担由此给甲方造成的损失。
EN: (3) If Party B is split, merged, or changes its domicile, it shall promptly inform Party A in writing. If Party B fails to inform Party A in a timely manner, causing difficulties in contract performance, Party A may suspend contract performance and require Party B to bear losses caused to Party A thereby.

<!-- id: p000563 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （4）甲方不得以行政区划调整、政府换届、机构或者职能调整以及相关责任人更替为由中止合同。
EN: (4) Party A shall not suspend the contract on the grounds of administrative division adjustments, government term changes, institutional or functional adjustments, or changes of relevant responsible persons.

<!-- id: p000564 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 16.3合同的终止
EN: 16.3 Termination of the contract

<!-- id: p000565 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （1）合同因有效期限届满而终止；
EN: (1) The contract terminates upon expiration of its validity period;

<!-- id: p000566 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （2）乙方未按合同约定履行，构成根本性违约的，甲方有权终止合同，并追究乙方的违约责任。
EN: (2) If Party B fails to perform as agreed in the contract and constitutes a fundamental breach, Party A has the right to terminate the contract and pursue Party B’s liability for breach.

<!-- id: p000567 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 16.4 涉及国家利益、社会公共利益的情形
EN: 16.4 Circumstances involving national interests or public interests

<!-- id: p000568 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 政府采购合同继续履行将损害国家利益和社会公共利益的，双方当事人应当变更、中止或者终止合同。有过错的一方应当承担赔偿责任，双方都有过错的，各自承担相应的责任。
EN: Where continued performance of a government procurement contract would harm national interests or public interests, both parties shall amend, suspend, or terminate the contract. The party at fault shall bear compensation liability; if both parties are at fault, each shall bear corresponding responsibilities.

<!-- id: p000569 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 17. 合同分包
EN: 17. Contract subcontracting

<!-- id: p000570 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 17.1 乙方不得将合同转包给其他供应商。涉及合同分包的，乙方应根据采购文件和投标（响应）文件规定进行合同分包。
EN: 17.1 Party B shall not subcontract the contract as a whole (transfer/sublet) to other suppliers. Where contract subcontracting is involved, Party B shall subcontract in accordance with the procurement documents and bidding (response) documents.

<!-- id: p000571 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 17.2 乙方执行政府采购政策向中小企业依法分包的，乙方应当按采购文件和投标（响应）文件签订分包意向协议，分包意向协议属于本合同组成部分。
EN: 17.2 Where Party B, in implementing government procurement policies, subcontracts to SMEs in accordance with law, Party B shall sign a subcontracting intention agreement in accordance with the procurement documents and bidding (response) documents; the subcontracting intention agreement constitutes part of this contract.

<!-- id: p000572 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 18. 不可抗力
EN: 18. Force majeure

<!-- id: p000573 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 18.1 不可抗力是指合同双方不能预见、不能避免且不能克服的客观情况。
EN: 18.1 Force majeure refers to objective circumstances that neither party to the contract can foresee, avoid, or overcome.

<!-- id: p000574 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 18.2 任何一方对由于不可抗力造成的部分或全部不能履行合同不承担违约责任。但迟延履行后发生不可抗力的，不能免除责任。
EN: 18.2 Neither party shall bear liability for breach of contract for partial or total non-performance caused by force majeure. However, where force majeure occurs after delayed performance, liability shall not be exempted.

<!-- id: p000575 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 18.3 遇有不可抗力的一方，应及时将事件情况以书面形式告知另一方，并在事件发生后及时向另一方提交合同不能履行或部分不能履行或需要延期履行的详细报告，以及证明不可抗力发生及其持续时间的证据。
EN: 18.3 The party encountering force majeure shall promptly notify the other party in writing of the circumstances of the event, and shall timely submit to the other party, after the event occurs, a detailed report on the contract’s inability to be performed, partial inability to be performed, or need for deferred performance, as well as evidence proving the occurrence of the force majeure and its duration.

<!-- id: p000576 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 19. 解决争议的方法
EN: 19. Methods for Resolving Disputes

<!-- id: p000577 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 19.1 因本合同及合同有关事项发生的争议，由甲乙双方友好协商解决。协商不成时，可以向有关组织申请调解。合同一方或双方不愿调解或调解不成的，可以通过仲裁或诉讼的方式解决争议。
EN: 19.1 Any disputes arising from this contract or matters related to this contract shall be resolved through friendly consultation between Parties A and B. If consultation fails, mediation may be sought from the relevant organization(s). If one or both parties are unwilling to mediate, or if mediation fails, disputes may be resolved through arbitration or litigation.

<!-- id: p000578 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 19.2 选择仲裁的，应在【政府采购合同专用条款】中明确仲裁机构及仲裁地；通过诉讼方式解决的，可以在【政府采购合同专用条款】中进一步约定选择与争议有实际联系的地点的人民法院管辖，但管辖法院的约定不得违反级别管辖和专属管辖的规定。
EN: 19.2 If arbitration is chosen, the arbitration institution and place of arbitration shall be specified in 【政府采购合同专用条款】; if litigation is chosen, the parties may further agree in 【政府采购合同专用条款】 to select a people’s court at a location that has an actual connection with the dispute, but the agreement on jurisdiction shall not violate the rules on hierarchical jurisdiction and exclusive jurisdiction.

<!-- id: p000579 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 19.3 如甲乙双方有争议的事项不影响合同其他部分的履行，在争议解决期间，合同其他部分应当继续履行。
EN: 19.3 If the matters in dispute between Parties A and B do not affect the performance of other parts of the contract, during the dispute resolution period, the other parts of the contract shall continue to be performed.

<!-- id: p000580 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 20. 政府采购政策
EN: 20. Government Procurement Policies

<!-- id: p000581 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 20.1 本合同应当按照规定执行政府采购政策。
EN: 20.1 This contract shall implement government procurement policies in accordance with applicable regulations.

<!-- id: p000582 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 20.2 本合同依法执行政府采购政策的方式和内容，属于合同履约验收的范围。甲乙双方未按规定要求执行政府采购政策造成损失的，有过错的一方应当承担赔偿责任，双方都有过错的，各自承担相应的责任。
EN: 20.2 The method and content of this contract’s implementation of government procurement policies in accordance with law fall within the scope of contract performance acceptance. Where losses are caused because Parties A and B fail to implement government procurement policies as required, the party at fault shall bear compensation liability; where both parties are at fault, each shall bear corresponding liability.

<!-- id: p000583 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 20.3 对于为落实中小企业支持政策，通过采购项目整体预留、设置采购包专门预留、要求以联合体形式参加或者合同分包等措施签订的采购合同，应当明确标注本合同为中小企业预留合同。其中，要求以联合体形式参加采购活动或者合同分包的，须将联合协议或者分包意向协议作为采购合同的组成部分。
EN: 20.3 For procurement contracts signed to implement SME support policies through measures such as overall reservation of procurement projects, setting aside reserved procurement packages, requiring participation in the form of a consortium, or subcontracting, it shall be clearly indicated that this contract is a contract reserved for SMEs. Where participation in procurement activities in the form of a consortium or subcontracting is required, the consortium agreement or subcontracting intention agreement shall be included as a constituent part of the procurement contract.

<!-- id: p000584 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 21. 法律适用
EN: 21. Applicable Law

<!-- id: p000585 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 21.1 本合同的订立、生效、解释、履行及与本合同有关的争议解决，均适用法律、行政法规。
EN: 21.1 The formation, effectiveness, interpretation, performance, and dispute resolution related to this contract shall all be governed by laws and administrative regulations.

<!-- id: p000586 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 21.2 本合同条款与法律、行政法规的强制性规定不一致的，双方当事人应按照法律、行政法规的强制性规定修改本合同的相关条款。
EN: 21.2 Where the terms of this contract are inconsistent with mandatory provisions of laws and administrative regulations, the parties shall amend the relevant terms of this contract in accordance with such mandatory provisions.

<!-- id: p000587 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 22. 通知
EN: 22. Notices

<!-- id: p000588 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 22.1 本合同任何一方向对方发出的通知、信件、数据电文等，应当发送至本合同第一部分《政府采购合同协议书》所约定的通讯地址、联系人、联系电话或电子邮箱。
EN: 22.1 Any notices, letters, data messages, etc. sent by either party to the other under this contract shall be sent to the mailing address, contact person, contact telephone number, or email address agreed in Part I, the “Government Procurement Contract Agreement,” of this contract.

<!-- id: p000589 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 22.2 一方当事人变更名称、住所、联系人、联系电话或电子邮箱等信息的，应当在变更后3日内及时书面通知对方，对方实际收到变更通知前的送达仍为有效送达。
EN: 22.2 Where a party changes its name, domicile, contact person, contact telephone number, email address, or other information, it shall promptly notify the other party in writing within 3 days after the change. Service made before the other party actually receives the change notice shall remain valid.

<!-- id: p000590 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 22.3本合同一方给另一方的通知均应采用书面形式，传真或快递送到本合同中规定的对方的地址和办理签收手续。
EN: 22.3 All notices given by one party to the other under this contract shall be in written form and shall be delivered by fax or courier to the other party’s address specified in this contract, with receipt-signing procedures completed.

<!-- id: p000591 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 22.4通知以送达之日或通知书中规定的生效之日起生效，两者中以较迟之日为准。
EN: 22.4 A notice shall take effect on the date of service or on the effective date specified in the notice, whichever is later.

<!-- id: p000592 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 合同未尽事项
EN: Matters Not Covered by the Contract

<!-- id: p000593 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 23.1合同未尽事项见【政府采购合同专用条款】。
EN: 23.1 Matters not covered by the contract are set forth in 【政府采购合同专用条款】.

<!-- id: p000594 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 23.2 合同附件与合同正文具有同等的法律效力。
EN: 23.2 Contract appendices have the same legal effect as the main text of the contract.

<!-- id: p000611 type: paragraph -->

<!-- id: p000614 type: paragraph -->

<!-- id: p000615 type: paragraph -->

<!-- id: p000616 type: paragraph -->

<!-- id: p000624 type: paragraph -->

EN: 2. For ease of reference, please arrange the contents of the bidding documents in the above order and indicate in the table of contents the starting page number for each item.

EN: Xinjiang Nengshi Construction Project Management Consulting Co., Ltd.:

<!-- id: p000628 type: paragraph -->
ZH: (投标人全称）授权(全权代表姓名）（职务、职称)为全权代表，参加贵方组织的（采购项目名称、采购编号）招标的有关活动，有能力提供项目中的货物及相关服务，并保证所提交的所有文件和说明是真实、有效和准确的。
EN: (Full name of bidder) authorizes (name of plenipotentiary representative) (position, professional title) as the plenipotentiary representative to participate in the activities related to the tender organized by your organization for (procurement project name, procurement number), has the capability to provide the goods and related services in the project, and guarantees that all documents and statements submitted are true, valid, and accurate.

<!-- id: p000629 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 为此我方同意在投标人须知前列表规定的投标日期起遵守本承诺函中的承诺且在投标有效期满之前均具有约束力。
EN: Accordingly, we agree that the commitments in this commitment letter shall be observed from the bid date specified in the front appendix to the Instructions to Bidders and shall remain binding until the bid validity period expires.

<!-- id: p000630 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 1、我方已详细阅读并理解了全部招标文件，包括招标的修改文件（如有的话）、参考资料及有关附件，确认无误，我们完全理解并同意放弃对这方面有不明及误解的权利。
EN: 1. We have carefully read and understood all tender documents, including any tender amendment documents (if any), reference materials, and relevant attachments, and confirm that there are no errors. We fully understand and agree to waive any right to claim lack of understanding or misunderstanding in this respect.

<!-- id: p000631 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2、我方承诺已经具备《中华人民共和国政府采购法》第二十二条中规定的参加政府采购活动的投标人应当具备的条件。
EN: 2. We commit that we already meet the conditions that bidders participating in government procurement activities shall have as stipulated in Article 22 of the Government Procurement Law of the People’s Republic of China.

<!-- id: p000632 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 3、提供投标须知规定的全部投标文件；投标保证金已交纳，本投标文件的有效期限为开标后  90 天。如果在招标后规定的投标有效期内撤回投标文件或者有其他违约行为， 我们的投标保证金可不予退还。
EN: 3. Provide all bidding documents as required in the Instructions to Bidders; the bid bond has been paid, and the validity period of this bidding document is  90 days after bid opening. If we withdraw the bidding documents within the bid validity period specified after tendering or commit any other breach, our bid bond may be forfeited and not refunded.

<!-- id: p000633 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4、保证遵守招标文件中的有关条款，执行双方所签订的合同，按期、按质、按量履行合同规定的责任和义务，提供设备，及其相关的运输、包装、运杂保险、装卸、安装、培训、售后服务等，并提供免费          年的质保。总价格及明细见明细报价表。
EN: 4. Guarantee to comply with the relevant terms in the tender documents, perform the contract signed by both parties, and fulfill the responsibilities and obligations stipulated in the contract on time, with required quality and quantity; provide equipment and related transportation, packaging, freight/miscellaneous insurance, loading/unloading, installation, training, after-sales service, etc., and provide a free warranty of          years. The total price and details are shown in the detailed quotation table.

<!-- id: p000634 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5、我方愿意向贵方提供真实完整的任何与该项目有关的数据、情况和技术 资料。并承诺一切证明材料的真实性。
EN: 5. We are willing to provide your organization with any true and complete data, information, and technical materials related to this project, and we commit to the authenticity of all supporting materials.

<!-- id: p000635 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 6、我们完全理解贵方不一定要接受最低报价及有权接受或拒绝所有的投标人。
EN: 6. We fully understand that your organization is not necessarily required to accept the lowest quotation and has the right to accept or reject all bidders.

<!-- id: p000636 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 7、若我方中标，愿意在签订合同时提交  甲乙双方协商  的履约保证金。
EN: 7. If we win the bid, we are willing to submit the performance bond to be negotiated by Parties A and B when signing the contract.

<!-- id: p000637 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 8、若我方中标，同意并接受招标文件要求的付款方式。
EN: 8. If we win the bid, we agree to and accept the payment method required by the tender documents.

<!-- id: p000638 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 9、若我方中标，我方愿意按有关规定支付招标服务费。
EN: 9. If we win the bid, we are willing to pay the tender service fee in accordance with relevant provisions.

<!-- id: p000639 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 10、我方将严格遵守《中华人民共和国政府采购法》第七十七条规定：投标人有下列情形之一的，处以采购金额5‰以上10‰以下的罚款，列入不良行为记录名单，在一至三年内禁止参加政府采购活动；有违法所得的，并处没收违法所得；情节严重的，由工商行政管理机关吊销营业执照；构成犯罪的，依法追究刑事责任：
EN: 10. We will strictly comply with Article 77 of the Government Procurement Law of the People’s Republic of China: Where a bidder has any of the following circumstances, it shall be fined not less than 5‰ and not more than 10‰ of the procurement amount, be included in the list of improper conduct records, and be prohibited from participating in government procurement activities for one to three years; where there are illegal gains, such gains shall be confiscated; where circumstances are serious, the business license shall be revoked by the administrative authority for industry and commerce; where a crime is constituted, criminal liability shall be pursued in accordance with law:

<!-- id: p000640 type: paragraph -->
ZH: (一）提供虚假材料谋取中标的；
EN: (1) Providing false materials to seek winning the bid;

<!-- id: p000641 type: paragraph -->
ZH: (二）采取不正当手段诋毁、排挤其他投标人的；
EN: (2) Using improper means to slander or exclude other bidders;

<!-- id: p000642 type: paragraph -->
ZH: (三）与采购单位、其它投标人或者釆购代理机构恶意串通的；
EN: (3) Maliciously colluding with the purchasing unit, other bidders, or the procurement agent;

<!-- id: p000643 type: paragraph -->
ZH: (四）向采购人、采购代理机构行贿或者提供其他不正当利益的；
EN: (4) Bribing the purchaser or the procurement agent, or providing other improper benefits;

<!-- id: p000644 type: paragraph -->
ZH: (五）在招标采购过程中与采购人进行协商的；
EN: (5) Conducting consultations with the purchaser during the tender procurement process;

<!-- id: p000645 type: paragraph -->
ZH: (六）拒绝有关部门监督检查或提供虚假情况的。
EN: (6) Refusing supervision/inspection by relevant authorities or providing false information.

<!-- id: p000772 type: paragraph -->

EN: This entity solemnly declares that, in accordance with the “Notice of the Ministry of Finance, the Ministry of Civil Affairs, and the China Disabled Persons’ Federation on Government Procurement Policies to Promote Employment of Persons with Disabilities” (Caiku [2017] No. 141), this entity is a qualified disabled persons’ welfare unit, and this entity participates in the procurement activity for the ______ project of the _ (purchaser) entity, providing goods manufactured by this entity (with the project undertaken/providing services by this entity), or providing goods manufactured by other disabled persons’ welfare units (excluding goods using trademarks registered by non-disabled persons’ welfare units).

<!-- id: p000773 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 本单位知悉《关于促进残疾人就业政府采购政策的通知》（财库〔2017〕141 号）的规定，承诺提供的声明函内容是真实的，如提供声明函内容不实，则依法追究相关法律责任。
EN: This entity is aware of the provisions of the “Notice on Government Procurement Policies to Promote Employment of Persons with Disabilities” (Caiku [2017] No. 141) and commits that the contents of the provided declaration letter are true. EN_ROW: | 11 | Agree that the purchaser may review and verify, in any form, the authenticity and validity of our bid/bid document contents. |  |  |

EN_ROW: | 13 | Other business terms deviation notes: |

<!-- id: p000811 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 注：：1.对于上述要求，如投标人完全响应，则请在“是否响应”栏内打“√”，对打“×”视为偏离，请在“偏离说明”栏内扼要说明偏离情况。
EN: Note:: 1. For the above requirements, if the bidder fully complies, please mark “√” in the “Whether compliant” column; marking “×” is deemed a deviation. Please briefly describe the deviation in the “Deviation explanation” column.

<!-- id: p000812 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2.投标人应认真填写本响应表，若评委会在评审期间，发现有虚假填写本响应表的，则将可能被视为存在两个投标方案，评委会将按本招标文件相关规定执行。
EN: 2. The bidder shall complete this response form carefully. If the evaluation committee finds any false entries during the review, it may be deemed that there are two bidding proposals, and the evaluation committee will act in accordance with the relevant provisions of this tender document.

<!-- id: p000813 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 3.本表内容不得擅自修改。
EN: 3. The contents of this table must not be altered without authorization.

<!-- id: p000817 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （十一）质量保证书
EN: (XI) Quality Guarantee Letter

<!-- id: p000818 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （采购人）：
EN: (Purchaser):

<!-- id: p000819 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 本质量保证书作为（投标人名称）参与（招标代理机构名称）组织的“  （项目名称）”的货物及服务采购，对所提供的货物设备的质量保证的证明。现郑重承诺提供以下质量保证并承担相应的法律责任：
EN: This Quality Guarantee Letter serves as proof of the quality guarantee for the goods and services procurement for “  (Project Name)” organized by (Tender Agency Name), in which (Bidder Name) participates, for the quality assurance of the goods and equipment provided. We hereby solemnly undertake to provide the following quality guarantees and assume corresponding legal responsibility:

<!-- id: p000820 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 1、提供的投标货物均是全新、制造厂商具有质量合格证和国家有关质量检测部门检测合格、手续齐全且合法的产品；
EN: 1. All bid goods provided are brand-new products, with the manufacturer’s certificate of quality conformity, have passed inspection by the relevant national quality inspection authorities, with complete formalities and lawful origin;

<!-- id: p000821 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2、提供的投标货物均是符合招标文件规定的质量、规格和要求的；
EN: 2. All bid goods provided comply with the quality, specifications, and requirements stipulated in the tender documents;

<!-- id: p000822 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 3、提供《售后服务承诺书》所承诺的全部服务项目；
EN: 3. Provide all service items committed in the “After-sales Service Commitment Letter”;

<!-- id: p000823 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4、若产品质量不合格或缺陷，作为货物的提供方，我方愿接受招标方及相关部门的处罚，一切费用和损失由我方承担。
EN: 4. If the product quality is unqualified or defective, as the supplier of the goods, we are willing to accept penalties from the tendering party and relevant departments; all costs and losses shall be borne by us.

<!-- id: p000824 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5、招标人从中标人所提供的产品中随机抽取产品送法定质量检测单位检测，不管检测产品是否合格，检测费用都由中标单位承担。如果检测产品结果为不合格或者低于招标文件参数要求，招标人取消中标人中标资格，所有造成的损失由中标人承担，包括对第三方的损失。
EN: 5. The tenderer will randomly select products from those provided by the winning bidder and send them to a statutory quality testing institution for inspection. Regardless of whether the tested products are qualified, the testing costs shall be borne by the winning bidder. If the test results are unqualified or fall below the parameter requirements of the tender documents, the tenderer will cancel the winning bidder’s award qualification, and all resulting losses shall be borne by the winning bidder, including losses to third parties.

<!-- id: p000825 type: paragraph -->

EN: Bidding unit: (full name) (seal)

EN: (e.g., various awards, certificates, and other supporting materials)

<!-- id: p000830 type: paragraph -->
ZH: （十三）投标单位反商业贿赂承诺书
EN: (XIII) Anti-commercial Bribery Commitment Letter of the Bidding Unit

ZH: 我公司承诺在UU（项目编号、项目名称）UU招标活动中，不给予国家工作人员以及中介机构工作人员及其亲属各种形式的商业贿赂（包括送礼金礼品、有价证券、购物券、回扣、佣金、咨询费、劳务费、赞助费、宣传费、支付旅游费用、报销各种消费凭证、宴请、娱乐等），如有上述行为，我公司及项目参与人员愿意按照《反不正当竞争法》的有关规定接受处罚。
EN: Our company commits that in the UU (project number, project name) UU tendering activities, we will not offer any form of commercial bribery to state personnel, intermediary agency staff, or their relatives (including gifts of cash or presents, securities, shopping vouchers, rebates, commissions, consulting fees, service fees, sponsorship fees, publicity fees, payment of travel expenses, reimbursement of various consumption vouchers, banquets, entertainment, etc.). If any of the above occurs, our company and project participants are willing to accept punishment in accordance with the relevant provisions of the Anti-Unfair Competition Law.

EN: If any of the above acts exist, our company and project participants voluntarily waive the bidding and quotation qualifications for this project; if we are a pre-award or transaction candidate, we also voluntarily waive the award/transaction qualification.

<!-- id: p000846 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 第七部分   评标办法和细则
EN: Part VII   Bid Evaluation Methods and Detailed Rules

<!-- id: p000847 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 根据《中华人民共和国政府采购法》、《政府采购货物和服务招标投标管理办法》 《评标委员会和评标方法暂行规定》以及国家和地方颁布的有关法令、法规，并结合本项目的实际，按照公正、公平、科学、择优的原则选择中标人，特制定本办法。
EN: In accordance with the PRC Government Procurement Law, the Administrative Measures for Bidding and Tendering of Government Procurement of Goods and Services, the Interim Provisions on Evaluation Committees and Evaluation Methods, as well as relevant national and local laws and regulations, and in light of the actual circumstances of this project, this method is formulated to select the winning bidder(s) in accordance with the principles of impartiality, fairness, scientific evaluation, and selection of the best.

<!-- id: p000848 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 一、总则
EN: I. General Provisions

<!-- id: p000849 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 1、评定总则和规定
EN: 1. General evaluation rules and provisions

<!-- id: p000850 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 1.1  为最大限度地保护各当事人的权益，评审小组应严格按照招标文件的要求进行评定，编制评标报告。评审人员必须严格遵守保密规定，不得泄漏评审有关的情况，不得索贿受贿，不得参加影响评审的任何活动。
EN: 1.1  To protect the rights and interests of all parties to the greatest extent, the evaluation panel shall conduct evaluation strictly in accordance with the requirements of the tender documents and prepare an evaluation report. Evaluators must strictly comply with confidentiality requirements, must not disclose any information related to the evaluation, must not solicit or accept bribes, and must not participate in any activities that affect the evaluation.

<!-- id: p000851 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 1.2  评审时，评审小组应当对照招标文件规定的条件和标准，对各投标人投标文件的合格性、完整性和有效性进行审查、比较和评估，其中对投标人的资格条件、主要技术参数、商务报价和其他评审要素等，评定人员应逐项进行审查、比较，不得漏评少评。如发现与招标文件要求相偏离的，应对其偏离情况进行必要的核实，并在工作底稿中予以说明；如属于实质性偏离或符合无效响应条件的，应当询问投标人，并允许投标人进行陈述申辩，但不允许其对实质性偏离条款进行补充、修正或撤回。
EN: 1.2  During evaluation, the evaluation panel shall, against the conditions and standards stipulated in the tender documents, review, compare, and assess the compliance, completeness, and validity of each bidder’s bid documents. For the bidder’s qualification conditions, main technical parameters, commercial quotation, and other evaluation factors, evaluators shall review and compare item by item, without omission or insufficient evaluation. If any deviation from the tender document requirements is found, the deviation shall be verified as necessary and explained in the working papers; if it constitutes a substantive deviation or meets the conditions for an invalid response, the bidder shall be questioned and allowed to make a statement and defense, but the bidder is not allowed to supplement, amend, or withdraw substantive deviation clauses.

<!-- id: p000852 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 1.3  评定原则：
EN: 1.3  Evaluation principles:

<!-- id: p000853 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 1.3.1 采取综合评分法。由评审小组采用综合评分法对提交有效报价的投标人的投标文件进行综合评分。综合评分法，是指投标文件满足招标文件全部实质性要求且按评审因素的量化指标评审得分最高的投标人为中标候选投标人的评审方法。
EN: 1.3.1 Adopt the comprehensive scoring method. The evaluation panel shall use the comprehensive scoring method to comprehensively score the bid documents of bidders who submit valid quotations. The comprehensive scoring method refers to the evaluation method in which the bidder whose bid documents meet all substantive requirements of the tender documents and obtains the highest score under the quantified indicators of the evaluation factors is determined as the winning candidate bidder.

<!-- id: p000854 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 1.3.2 评审小组应当根据综合评分情况，按照评审得分由高到低顺序推荐3 名以上中标候选投标人，并编写评标报告。评审得分相同的，按照最后报价由低到高的顺序推荐。评审得分且最后报价相同的，由评审小组确定以按照技术指标优劣顺序或抽签确定排名先后推荐。
EN: 1.3.2 The evaluation panel shall, based on the comprehensive scoring results, recommend 3 or more winning candidate bidders in descending order of evaluation score and prepare an evaluation report. Where evaluation scores are the same, recommendations shall be made in ascending order of the final quotation (from low to high). Where both the evaluation score and the final quotation are the same, the evaluation panel shall determine the ranking and recommendation order either according to the relative merits of technical indicators or by drawing lots.

<!-- id: p000855 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 1.4  本评标办法仅适用于本次招标。
EN: 1.4  This bid evaluation method applies only to this tender.

<!-- id: p000856 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 二、机构组成和职能
EN: II. Organizational composition and functions

<!-- id: p000857 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 本次招标将设监督小组、组织机构和评审小组。
EN: This tender will establish a supervision group, an organizing body, and an evaluation panel.

<!-- id: p000858 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2.1  监督小组机构组成和职能
EN: 2.1  Composition and functions of the supervision group

<!-- id: p000859 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2.1.1  机构成员：由招标人相关部门组成。
EN: 2.1.1  Members: composed of relevant departments of the tenderer.

<!-- id: p000860 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2.1.2  职能：独立行使监督工作，对所有招标工作做出复审意见。
EN: 2.1.2  Functions: independently exercise supervision and provide review opinions on all tendering work.

<!-- id: p000861 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2.2  组织机构的组成和职能
EN: 2.2  Composition and functions of the organizing body

<!-- id: p000862 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2.2.1 机构成员：由本项目采购代理机构相关人员组成。
EN: 2.2.1 Members: composed of relevant personnel of the procurement agent for this project.

<!-- id: p000863 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2.2.2 职能：按规定的程序和要求依法严密组织招标、评定等各项活动，且客观如实予以记录和反映，对评审小组的评分记录，评定过程中不干扰和影响评审小组正常的评定工作。
EN: 2.2.2 Functions: Organize tendering, evaluation, and other activities in a lawful and rigorous manner according to the prescribed procedures and requirements, and record and reflect them objectively and truthfully; for the evaluation panel’s scoring records, do not interfere with or affect the evaluation panel’s normal evaluation work during the evaluation process.

<!-- id: p000864 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2.3 评审小组组成和职能
EN: 2.3 Composition and functions of the evaluation panel

<!-- id: p000865 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2.3.1 评审小组由相关行业专家及采购人代表共5人组成，其中业主代表1人，在新疆政府采购网专家库中随机抽取相关技术、经济类专业4人。
EN: 2.3.1 The evaluation panel consists of 5 persons in total, including relevant industry experts and a purchaser’s representative, among whom there is 1 owner’s representative and 4 technical/economic professionals randomly selected from the expert pool of the Xinjiang Government Procurement Website.

<!-- id: p000866 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2.3.2 职能：根据招标文件的要求，对投标文件进行初步检查、汇总、分析和比较，并做好记录；对合格的投标人提出投标文件中需要澄清的问题。对不合格的投标人说明原因；对合格的投标文件认真、客观、公正地评审；对合格的投标人进行评定；完成所评审项目的评定报告，评审小组按评定原则推荐中标候选人。
EN: 2.3.2 Functions: In accordance with the requirements of the tender documents, conduct a preliminary inspection, compilation, analysis, and comparison of bid documents and keep records; raise clarification questions in the bid documents to qualified bidders. Explain the reasons to unqualified bidders; carefully, objectively, and impartially review qualified bid documents; evaluate qualified bidders; complete the evaluation report for the reviewed project, and recommend winning candidates according to the evaluation principles.

<!-- id: p000867 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2.3.3 评审小组应当对照招标文件规定的条件和标准，对各投标人投标文件的合格性、完整性和有效性进行审查、比较和评估，其中对投标人的资格条件、主要技术参数、商务报价和其他评审要素等，评审专家应逐项进行审查、比较，不得漏评少评。如发现与采购文件要求相偏离的，应对其偏离情形进行必要的核实，并在评审报告中予以说明；如属于实质性偏离或符合无效响应条件的，应当询问投标人，并允许投标人进行陈述申辩，但不允许其对偏离条款时行补充、修正或撤回。
EN: 2.3.3 The evaluation panel shall, against the conditions and standards stipulated in the tender documents, review, compare, and assess the compliance, completeness, and validity of each bidder’s bid documents. For the bidder’s qualification conditions, main technical parameters, commercial quotation, and other evaluation factors, evaluation experts shall review and compare item by item, without omission or insufficient evaluation. If any deviation from the procurement document requirements is found, the deviation shall be verified as necessary and explained in the evaluation report; if it constitutes a substantive deviation or meets the conditions for an invalid response, the bidder shall be questioned and allowed to make a statement and defense, but the bidder is not allowed to supplement, amend, or withdraw the deviation clauses.

<!-- id: p000868 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2.3.4 各评审小组成员的评分情况和评审意见由采购代理机构审查，如发现评审小组的评审意见带有明显倾向性，或不按规定程序和标准评审、计分的，必须要求评审小组进行书面澄清和说明。
EN: 2.3.4 The procurement agent shall examine the scoring and evaluation opinions of each evaluation panel member. If the panel’s evaluation opinions show obvious bias, or if evaluation/scoring is not conducted according to the prescribed procedures and standards, the panel must be required to provide written clarification and explanation.

<!-- id: p000869 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2.3.5 评审小组成员在评定过程中不得将自己的观点，强加给其他评审人员，评审小组人员应自主发表见解，对评审意见承担个人责任。各评审人员应当独立、客观、公正地提出评审意见，不得带有倾向性，不得影响其他人员评审，并在评标报告上签字；如对评标报告有异议的，可以在报告上签署不同意见，并说明理由，否则将视为同意。
EN: 2.3.5 During the evaluation process, evaluation panel members must not impose their views on other evaluators. Panel members shall express their opinions independently and bear personal responsibility for their evaluation opinions. Evaluators shall independently, objectively, and impartially provide evaluation opinions without bias, shall not influence other evaluators’ reviews, and shall sign the evaluation report; if they dissent from the evaluation report, they may sign a dissenting opinion on the report and state reasons, otherwise they will be deemed to agree.

<!-- id: p000870 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2.3.6 各评审小组成员要配合采购代理机构单位答复投标人提出的质疑，配合财政部门的投诉处理工作。
EN: 2.3.6 Each evaluation panel member shall cooperate with the procurement agent in responding to bidders’ queries and cooperate with the finance authority’s complaint handling work.

<!-- id: p000871 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2.3.7 评定委员会成员有如下行为之一的，责令改正，给予警告，可以并处一千元以下的罚款：
EN: 2.3.7 If an evaluation committee member commits any of the following acts, they shall be ordered to make corrections, given a warning, and may be fined up to 1,000 yuan:

<!-- id: p000872 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 1）明知应当回避而未主动回避的；
EN: 1) Knowing they should recuse themselves but failing to do so proactively;

<!-- id: p000873 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2）在知道自己为评审小组身份后至评定结束前的时段内私下接触供应商的；
EN: 2) Privately contacting suppliers during the period after knowing they are an evaluation panel member and before the end of the evaluation;

<!-- id: p000874 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 3）在评定过程中擅离职守，影响评定程序正常进行的；
EN: 3) Leaving their post without authorization during the evaluation, affecting the normal progress of the evaluation procedure;

<!-- id: p000875 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4）在评定过程有明显不合理或者不正当倾向性的；
EN: 4) Having an obviously unreasonable or improper bias during the evaluation process;

<!-- id: p000876 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5）未按招标文件规定的评定方法和标准进行评定的。
EN: 5) Failing to conduct evaluation in accordance with the evaluation method and standards stipulated in the tender documents.

<!-- id: p000877 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 三、评标原则
EN: III. Bid evaluation principles

<!-- id: p000878 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 3.1评标遵循公平、公正、科学、择优的原则。
EN: 3.1 Bid evaluation follows the principles of fairness, impartiality, scientific evaluation, and selection of the best.

<!-- id: p000879 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 3.2对所有投标人的投标评估，都采用相同的程序和标准。
EN: 3.2 The same procedures and standards are applied to the evaluation of bids from all bidders.

<!-- id: p000880 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 3.3评标将严格按照招标文件的要求和评标标准及办法进行。
EN: 3.3 Bid evaluation will be conducted strictly in accordance with the requirements of the tender documents and the evaluation standards and methods.

<!-- id: p000881 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 3.4根据招标文件规定的各项评价标准通过评审打分排序推荐出1-3名中标候选人。
EN: 3.4 According to the evaluation criteria stipulated in the tender documents, the committee will score, rank, and recommend 1–3 winning candidates.

<!-- id: p000882 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 3.5评标委员会判断投标文件的响应性仅基于投标文件本身而不靠外部证据。
EN: 3.5 The bid evaluation committee’s determination of the responsiveness of bid documents is based solely on the bid documents themselves and not on external evidence.

<!-- id: p000883 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 3.6评标委员会拒绝被确定为非实质性响应的投标，投标人不能通过修正或撤销不符之处而使其投标成为实质性响应的投标。
EN: 3.6 The bid evaluation committee rejects bids determined to be non-substantively responsive; bidders cannot make their bids substantively responsive by correcting or withdrawing nonconformities.

<!-- id: p000884 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 四、评标纪律
EN: IV. Bid evaluation discipline

<!-- id: p000885 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.1评标委员会成员应当客观、公正地履行职责，遵守职业道德，对所提出的评审意见承担个人责任；
EN: 4.1 Members of the bid evaluation committee shall perform their duties objectively and impartially, abide by professional ethics, and bear personal responsibility for the evaluation opinions they provide;

<!-- id: p000886 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.2评标委员会成员和与评标活动有关的工作人员不得向任何投标人或与评标工作无关的人员透露与评标有关的任何情况；
EN: 4.2 Members of the bid evaluation committee and staff related to the evaluation activities must not disclose any information related to bid evaluation to any bidder or any person unrelated to the evaluation work;

<!-- id: p000887 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.3封闭评标期间，评委不得独自与外界接触，个人的通讯工具均应交由招标监督人员集中保管。需要和外部联系应通过招标监督人员联系。
EN: 4.3 During the closed evaluation period, evaluators must not contact the outside world alone; personal communication devices shall be handed over to the tender supervision personnel for centralized safekeeping. Any need to contact the outside shall be arranged through the tender supervision personnel.

<!-- id: p000888 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4.4评标期间，投标人应服从工作人员的指挥，不得出现干扰评标工作的正常进行或影响评标公正性的现象，否则，将视为废标。
EN: 4.4 During bid evaluation, bidders shall obey the staff’s instructions and must not interfere with the normal conduct of bid evaluation work or affect the fairness of bid evaluation; otherwise, the bid will be deemed invalid.

<!-- id: p000889 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 五、评定程序
EN: V. Evaluation procedures

<!-- id: p000890 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.1  初步评审及报价复核
EN: 5.1  Preliminary review and quotation recheck

<!-- id: p000891 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.1.1初步评审将对开标时有效的投标文件进行,根据招标文件,审查并逐项列出投标文件的全部投标重大偏差。
EN: 5.1.1 The preliminary review will be conducted on bid documents that are valid at the time of bid opening. In accordance with the tender documents, it will review and list item by item all major bid deviations in the bid documents.

<!-- id: p000892 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.1.2下列情况属于重大偏差：
EN: 5.1.2 The following circumstances constitute major deviations:

<!-- id: p000893 type: paragraph -->
ZH: (1)未按文件要求的规定提交投标保证金或者所提供的投标担保有瑕疵的；
EN: (1) Failure to submit the bid security as required by the documents, or the bid guarantee provided has defects;

<!-- id: p000894 type: paragraph -->
ZH: (2)无法定代表人出具的授权委托书的；
EN: (2) No power of attorney issued by the legal representative;

<!-- id: p000895 type: paragraph -->
ZH: (3)无单位盖章并无法定代表人或法定代表人授权的代理人签字或盖章；
EN: (3) No unit seal and no signature or seal of the legal representative or an agent authorized by the legal representative;

<!-- id: p000896 type: paragraph -->
ZH: (4)不具备招标文件中规定的资格要求的；
EN: (4) Not meeting the qualification requirements specified in the tender documents;

<!-- id: p000897 type: paragraph -->
ZH: (5)报价超过招标文件中预算金额或最高限价的；
EN: (5) Quotation exceeds the budget amount or maximum price limit in the tender documents;

<!-- id: p000898 type: paragraph -->
ZH: (6)投标文件载明的招标项目完成期限超过招标文件规定的期限；
EN: (6) The completion period for the tender project stated in the bid documents exceeds the period specified in the tender documents;

<!-- id: p000899 type: paragraph -->
ZH: (7)投标人名称或组织结构与购买招标文件时不一致且未提供有效证明；
EN: (7) The bidder’s name or organizational structure is inconsistent with that at the time of purchasing the tender documents and no valid proof is provided;

<!-- id: p000900 type: paragraph -->
ZH: (8)法定代表人为同一个人的两个及两个以上法人，母公司、全资子公司及其控股公司，在同一货物采购中同时投标。
EN: (8) Two or more legal persons with the same legal representative, or a parent company, its wholly-owned subsidiary, and its holding company, bid simultaneously in the same goods procurement.

<!-- id: p000901 type: paragraph -->
ZH: (9)投标有效期不满足招标文件要求的；
EN: (9) The bid validity period does not meet the requirements of the tender documents;

<!-- id: p000902 type: paragraph -->
ZH: (10)对招标文件主要条款和承诺存在重大出入或保留；
EN: (10) Major discrepancies or reservations regarding the main clauses and commitments in the tender documents;

<!-- id: p000903 type: paragraph -->
ZH: (11)投标人以行贿手段谋取成交或者以其他弄虚作假方式投标，违反招标纪律的；相互串标，排挤其他投标人的不公平竞争，损害采购人或其他投标人的合法权益的。
EN: (11) The bidder seeks award by bribery or bids by other fraudulent means, violating tender discipline; colludes with others to rig bids, engages in unfair competition to squeeze out other bidders, and harms the lawful rights and interests of the purchaser or other bidders.

<!-- id: p000904 type: paragraph -->
ZH: (12)扰乱会场秩序经劝阻无效的。
EN: (12) Disrupting order at the venue and failing to stop after being urged to do so.

<!-- id: p000905 type: paragraph -->
ZH: (13)投标文件含有采购人不能接受的附加条件的；
EN: (13) The bid documents contain additional conditions unacceptable to the purchaser;

<!-- id: p000906 type: paragraph -->
ZH: (14)法律、法规和招标文件规定的其他无效情形。
EN: (14) Other invalid circumstances stipulated by laws, regulations, and the tender documents.

<!-- id: p000907 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.1.3 投标文件有上述重大偏差之一的，为未能对招标文件做出实质性响应，作废标处理，不再进入以后的评标程序。
EN: 5.1.3 If the bid documents have any of the above major deviations, they are deemed to have failed to substantively respond to the tender documents and will be treated as invalid bids, and will not enter the subsequent bid evaluation procedures.

<!-- id: p000908 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.1.4 细微偏差是指投标文件在实质上响应招标文件要求，但在个别地方存在漏项或者提供了不完整的技术信息和数据等情况，并且补正这些遗漏或者不完整不会对其他投标人造成不公平结果。细微偏差不影响投标文件的有效性。
EN: 5.1.4 Minor deviations refer to cases where the bid documents substantively respond to the requirements of the tender documents, but there are omissions in individual places or incomplete technical information and data, and correcting such omissions or incompleteness will not cause an unfair result to other bidders. Minor deviations do not affect the validity of the bid documents.

<!-- id: p000909 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.1.5 评标委员会应当书面要求存在细微偏差的投标人在评标结果前予以补正。
EN: 5.1.5 The bid evaluation committee shall require, in writing, bidders with minor deviations to make corrections before the evaluation results are issued.

<!-- id: p000910 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.1.6 计算错误将按以下方法更正：若按单价计算的结果与总价不一致，以单价为准修改总价；若用文字表示的数值与用数字表示的数值不一致，以文字表示的数值为准。如果投标人不接受对其错误的更正，其投标将被拒绝。
EN: 5.1.6 Calculation errors will be corrected as follows: if the result calculated by unit price is inconsistent with the total price, the unit price shall prevail and the total price shall be revised accordingly; if the value expressed in words is inconsistent with the value expressed in digits, the value expressed in words shall prevail. If the bidder does not accept the correction of its errors, its bid will be rejected.

<!-- id: p000911 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.1.7 评标委员会可以书面方式要求投标人对投标文件中含义不明确、对同类问题表述不一致或者有明显文字和计算错误的内容作必要的澄清、说明或者补正。澄清、说明或者补正应以书面方式进行并不得超出投标文件的范围或者改变投标的实质性内容。拒不按照要求对投标文件进行澄清、说明或者补正的，评标委员会可以否决其投标，作
EN: 5.1.7 The bid evaluation committee may, in writing, require the bidder to make necessary clarifications, explanations, or corrections to contents in the bid documents that are unclear in meaning, inconsistent in description of similar issues, or contain obvious textual and calculation errors. Clarifications, explanations, or corrections shall be made in writing and shall not go beyond the scope of the bid documents or change the substantive content of the bid. If the bidder refuses to clarify, explain, or correct the bid documents as required, the bid evaluation committee may reject its bid, to

<!-- id: p000912 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 废标处理。
EN: be treated as an invalid bid.

<!-- id: p000913 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.1.8 评标委员会判断投标文件的响应程度仅基于投标文件本身，而不靠外部证据。
EN: 5.1.8 The bid evaluation committee’s judgment of the degree of responsiveness of bid documents is based solely on the bid documents themselves and not on external evidence.

<!-- id: p000914 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.1.9 在评标过程中，评标委员会发现投标人以他人的名义投标、串通投标、以行贿手段谋取中标或者以其它弄虚作假方式投标的,该投标将作废标处理。
EN: 5.1.9 During the bid evaluation process, if the bid evaluation committee finds that a bidder has bid in another person’s name, colluded in bidding, sought to win the bid by bribery, or bid by other fraudulent means, the bid will be treated as invalid.

<!-- id: p000915 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.1.10 评标委员会经评审，认为所有投标都不符合招标文件要求的或所有投标报价均过高时，可以否决所有投标。评标委员会经评审，认定投标人以低于成本报价竟标的，其投标将作废标处理。
EN: 5.1.10 After evaluation, if the bid evaluation committee believes that all bids do not meet the requirements of the tender documents, or all bid quotations are excessively high, it may reject all bids. If, after evaluation, the bid evaluation committee determines that a bidder has bid at a price below cost, its bid will be treated as invalid.

<!-- id: p000916 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.1.11 经过初步评审，如果由于有效投标不足三家使得投标明显缺乏竞争的，评标委员会可以否决全部投标。
EN: 5.1.11 After the preliminary review, if the number of valid bids is less than three, resulting in an obvious lack of competition, the bid evaluation committee may reject all bids.

<!-- id: p000917 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.2  详细评审
EN: 5.2  Detailed review

<!-- id: p000918 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 经初步评审合格的投标文件，评标委员会将对投标文件按评分标准进行进一步评审、比较。
EN: For bid documents that pass the preliminary review, the bid evaluation committee will further review and compare the bid documents according to the scoring criteria.

<!-- id: p000919 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.3  评分办法
EN: 5.3  Scoring method

<!-- id: p000920 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.3.1 经济标30分，商务技术部分70分。
EN: 5.3.1 Economic section: 30 points; commercial and technical section: 70 points.

<!-- id: p000921 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.3.2 价格调整原则
EN: 5.3.2 Price adjustment principles

<!-- id: p000922 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 1）投标人的报价必须包含供货范围内所有内容。
EN: 1) The bidder’s quotation must include all contents within the scope of supply.

<!-- id: p000923 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2）投标人必须根据招标文件要求和产品技术状况列出质量保证期内所需备品备件的清单和价格，并将该备品备件价计入投标总价，若所提供的产品不需备品备件或免费提供，应在投标文件中说明。否则按漏项处理。
EN: 2) The bidder must, according to the requirements of the tender documents and the technical condition of the product, list the spare parts required during the quality warranty period and their prices, and include the spare parts cost in the total bid price. If the provided product does not require spare parts or spare parts will be provided free of charge, it shall be stated in the bid documents. Otherwise, it will be treated as an omission.

<!-- id: p000924 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 3）投标人报价如有漏项，则须将其他投标人报价中该项价格的最高价加计入该投标人的投标总价。
EN: 3) If the bidder’s quotation has omissions, the highest price of that item among other bidders’ quotations shall be added to the bidder’s total bid price.

<!-- id: p000925 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 4）调整后的价格作为投标人的评标价。根据评标价测算各投标人的经济标分值。
EN: 4) The adjusted price will be used as the bidder’s evaluation price. Economic scores for each bidder will be calculated based on the evaluation price.

<!-- id: p000926 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 5.3.3 经济标不设标底，依照如下标准计算报价得分：
EN: 5.3.3 The economic section has no base price and the quotation score is calculated according to the following standards:

<!-- id: p000927 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 1) 基准价为合理低价，即满足招标文件要求且投标价格最低的投标报价为评标基准价，其价格分为满分。其他投标投标人的价格分统一按照下列公式计算：
EN: 1) The benchmark price is a reasonable low price, i.e., the lowest bid quotation that meets the tender document requirements is the evaluation benchmark price, and its price score is full marks. The price scores of other bidders are calculated uniformly according to the following formula:

<!-- id: p000928 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 投标报价得分=(评标基准价／投标报价)×价格分值×100% ，结果保留两位小数。
EN: Bid quotation score = (evaluation benchmark price／bid quotation) × price score value × 100%, with the result retained to two decimal places.

<!-- id: p000929 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 2) 如果得分为负分时,按零分计。
EN: 2) If the calculated score is negative, it will be counted as zero.

<!-- id: p000930 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 六、其它注意事项
EN: VI. Other matters for attention

<!-- id: p000931 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 6.1  投标时，投标人应派代表在指定的地点参加投标。投标人人员必须及时解释和
EN: 6.1  When bidding, the bidder shall send a representative to participate at the designated location. The bidder’s personnel must promptly explain and

<!-- id: p000932 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 澄清投标文件内容，并以书面的形式签署确定等。
EN: clarify the contents of the bid documents, and confirm them by signing in written form, etc.

<!-- id: p000933 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 6.2  评审时如发现投标人的报价明显高于其市场报价或低于成本价的，应要求该投标人书面说明并提供相关证明材料。该投标人不能合理说明原因并提供证明材料的，评审小组应将该投标人的采购投标文件作无效处理，同时采购组织机构应将该情况报同级财政部门，并视情将其列入不良投标人名单。
EN: 6.2  If, during evaluation, a bidder’s quotation is found to be obviously higher than its market quotation or lower than cost, the bidder shall be required to provide a written explanation and relevant supporting materials. If the bidder cannot reasonably explain the reasons and provide supporting materials, the evaluation panel shall treat the bidder’s procurement bid documents as invalid; meanwhile, the procurement organizing body shall report the situation to the finance authority at the same level, and may list the bidder in the roster of bad bidders as appropriate.

<!-- id: p000934 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 七、详细评审附表
EN: VII. Detailed review appendices

<!-- id: p000935 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 附表1：符合性审查表
EN: Appendix 1: Compliance review checklist

<!-- id: t000306 type: table_row -->

<!-- id: t000307 type: table_row -->

<!-- id: t000312 type: table_row -->

EN_ROW: | 8 | Two or more legal persons with the same legal representative, or a parent company, its wholly-owned subsidiary, and its holding company, have not bid simultaneously in the same goods procurement. |

<!-- id: t000314 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: | 9 | 投标有效期满足招标文件要求的； |
EN_ROW: | 9 | The bid validity period meets the requirements of the tender documents; |

<!-- id: t000315 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: | 10 | 对招标文件主要条款和承诺未存在重大出入或保留； |
EN_ROW: | 10 | There are no major discrepancies or reservations regarding the main clauses and commitments in the tender documents; |

<!-- id: t000316 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: | 11 | 法律、法规和招标文件规定的其他无效情形。 |
EN_ROW: | 11 | Other invalid circumstances stipulated by laws, regulations, and the tender documents. |

<!-- id: p000936 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 特别说明：如投标人的投标文件中没有按此表的内容提供相关证明文件（如无特别要求，均提供复印件）或不符合上述审查内容的任意一条，其投标文件将视为无效投标文件。
EN: Special note: If the bidder’s bid documents do not provide the relevant supporting documents according to this table (unless otherwise specified, copies are provided) or fail to meet any of the above review items, the bid documents will be deemed invalid.

<!-- id: p000937 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 本项目采用综合评分法，核心产品为网络空间安全教学平台，提供相同品牌产品且通过资格审查、符合性审查的不同投标人参加同一合同项下投标的，按一家投标人计算，评审后得分最高的同品牌投标人获得中标人推荐资格；评审得分相同的，推荐报价低的投标人。
EN: This project adopts the comprehensive scoring method. The core product is the cyberspace security teaching platform. Where different bidders providing products of the same brand pass the qualification review and compliance review and participate in bidding under the same contract, they shall be counted as one bidder; after evaluation, the bidder of the same brand with the highest score obtains the recommended winner qualification; where evaluation scores are the same, the bidder with the lower quotation is recommended.

<!-- id: p000938 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 附表2：经济标得分（30分）
EN: Appendix 2: Economic section score (30 points)

<!-- id: t000317 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: | 序号 | 评审项目 | 分值 | 评分标准 |
EN_ROW: | No. | Evaluation item | Points | Scoring criteria |

<!-- id: t000318 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: | 1 | 投标报价 | 30分 | (评标基准价/投标报价)×30×100%，（小数点保留两位）<br/>评标基准价：以满足招标文件要求且投标价格最低的有效投标报价为评标基准价，其价格分为满分。其他投标人的价格统一按上述投标报价公式计算。 |
EN_ROW: | 1 | Bid quotation | 30 points | (evaluation benchmark price/bid quotation) × 30 × 100% (two decimal places retained)<br/>Evaluation benchmark price: The valid bid quotation that meets the tender document requirements and has the lowest bid price is taken as the evaluation benchmark price, and its price score is full marks. The prices of other bidders are calculated uniformly according to the above bid quotation formula. |

<!-- id: p000939 type: paragraph -->
ZH: 附表3、商务技术评审表（70分）
EN: Appendix 3: Commercial and technical evaluation table (70 points)

<!-- id: t000319 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: | 项目 | 评审内容 | 分值<br/>（分） |
EN_ROW: | Item | Evaluation content | Points<br/>(points) |

<!-- id: t000320 type: table_row -->
ZH_ROW: | 投标人相关资质证书 | 投标人具备ISO27001（信息安全管理体系）认证、ISO9001（质量管理体系）认证、CCRC信息系统安全运维服务资质、ITSS信息技术服务运行维护证书。每提供1个证书得0.5分，本项最高得2分，未提供得0分。 | 2 |
EN_ROW: | Bidder-related qualification certificates | The bidder has ISO27001 (Information Security Management System) certification, ISO9001 (Quality Management System) certification, CCRC information system security operations and maintenance service qualification, and ITSS information technology service operations and maintenance certificate. Each certificate provided scores 0.5 points; the maximum for this item is 2 points; if not provided, 0 points. | 2 |
